python3\n\"\"\"\nComplete pipeline for truth analysis probing on Qwen2.5-1.5B.\nStep 1: Generate behavioral labels by running model on TruthfulQA questions.\nStep 2: Extract activations from all layers.\nStep 3: Train linear probes across layers and token aggregation strategies.\nStep 4: Evaluate, visualize, and save best probe.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport json\nimport os\nimport pickle\nimport sys\nimport time\nimport re\nimport numpy as np\nimport torch\nfrom pathlib import Path\nfrom transformers import AutoModelForCausalLM, AutoTokenizer, AutoModel\nfrom sklearn.linear_model import LogisticRegression\nfrom sklearn.model_selection import cross_val_score, StratifiedKFold\nfrom sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler\nfrom sklearn.metrics import (\n    accuracy_score, precision_recall_fscore_support,\n    roc_auc_score, classification_report, roc_curve\n)\nimport matplotlib\nmatplotlib.use('Agg')\nimport matplotlib.pyplot as plt\n\nWORK_DIR = Path(\"/iopsstor/scratch/cscs/oyasunaga/autointerp_runs/jobs/truth_analysis_Qwen_Qwen2.5-1.5B_2513489\")\nMODEL_NAME = \"Qwen/Qwen2.5-1.5B\"\nDATA_FILE = WORK_DIR / \"labeled_data.jsonl\"\nBEHAVIORAL_LABELS_FILE = WORK_DIR / \"behavioral_labels.jsonl\"\nFINAL_PROBE_DIR = WORK_DIR / \"final_probe\"\nMETRICS_FILE = WORK_DIR / \"metrics.json\"\n\nos.makedirs(FINAL_PROBE_DIR, exist_ok=True)\n\n\ndef load_data():\n    \"\"\"Load labeled data from jsonl.\"\"\"\n    data = []\n    with open(DATA_FILE, 'r') as f:\n        for line in f:\n            data.append(json.loads(line))\n    return data\n\n\ndef normalize_text(text):\n    \"\"\"Normalize text for comparison.\"\"\"\n    text = text.lower().strip()\n    # Remove punctuation at end\n    text = re.sub(r'[.,;:!?\\s]+$', '', text)\n    # Remove articles at start\n    text = re.sub(r'^(the|a|an)\\s+', '', text)\n    return text\n\n\ndef check_answer_correctness(model_response, correct_answers):\n    \"\"\"\n    Check if the model's response matches any correct answer.\n    Uses flexible matching: checks if any correct answer is contained\n    in the model response or vice versa.\n    \"\"\"\n    response_lower = model_response.lower().strip()\n    response_normalized = normalize_text(response_lower)\n\n    for correct in correct_answers:\n        correct_lower = correct.lower().strip()\n        correct_normalized = normalize_text(correct_lower)\n\n        # Direct containment check\n        if correct_normalized in response_normalized:\n            return True\n        if response_normalized in correct_normalized:\n            return True\n\n        # Check key phrases (extract important words)\n        # Split correct answer into significant words (>3 chars)\n        key_words = [w for w in correct_normalized.split() if len(w) > 3]\n        if len(key_words) >= 2:\n            matches = sum(1 for w in key_words if w in response_normalized)\n            if matches >= len(key_words) * 0.6:\n                return True\n\n    return False\n\n\ndef generate_behavioral_labels(data, tokenizer, model):\n    \"\"\"\n    Generate behavioral labels by running the model on each question.\n    label=1 if model answers correctly, label=0 if incorrect.\n    \"\"\"\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n    print(\"STEP 1: Generating behavioral labels\")\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n\n    model.eval()\n    labels = []\n    correct_count = 0\n\n    for i, item in enumerate(data):\n        question = item['text']\n        correct_answers = item['correct_answers']\n\n        # Format as a simple Q&A prompt\n        prompt = f\"Q: {question}\\nA:\"\n\n        inputs = tokenizer(prompt, return_tensors=\"pt\", truncation=True, max_length=256)\n        inputs = {k: v.cuda() for k, v in inputs.items()}\n\n        with torch.no_grad():\n            outputs = model.generate(\n                **inputs,\n                max_new_tokens=100,\n                do_sample=False,\n                temperature=1.0,\n                pad_token_id=tokenizer.eos_token_id,\n            )\n\n        # Decode only the generated part\n        input_len = inputs['input_ids'].shape[1]\n        generated = tokenizer.decode(outputs[0][input_len:], skip_special_tokens=True).strip()\n\n        # Check correctness\n        is_correct = check_answer_correctness(generated, correct_answers)\n        label = 1 if is_correct else 0\n        labels.append(label)\n\n        if is_correct:\n            correct_count += 1\n\n        if i < 10 or (i < 100 and i % 20 == 0) or i % 100 == 0:\n            print(f\"\\n[{i}/{len(data)}] Q: {question[:80]}...\")\n            print(f\"  Generated: {generated[:120]}...\")\n            print(f\"  Correct answers: {correct_answers[0][:80]}...\")\n            print(f\"  Label: {label} ({'correct' if label else 'incorrect'})\")\n\n    print(f\"\\n{'=' * 40}\")\n    print(f\"Total correct: {correct_count}/{len(data)} ({correct_count/len(data)*100:.1f}%)\")\n    print(f\"Total incorrect: {len(data) - correct_count}/{len(data)} ({(len(data)-correct_count)/len(data)*100:.1f}%)\")\n\n    return labels\n\n\ndef save_behavioral_labels(data, labels):\n    \"\"\"Save behavioral labels to jsonl.\"\"\"\n    with open(BEHAVIORAL_LABELS_FILE, 'w') as f:\n        for item, label in zip(data, labels):\n            entry = {\"text\": item['text'], \"label\": label}\n            f.write(json.dumps(entry) + '\\n')\n    print(f\"Saved behavioral labels to {BEHAVIORAL_LABELS_FILE}\")\n\n\ndef extract_activations_all_layers(base_model, tokenizer, texts, aggregation='mean', batch_size=16):\n    \"\"\"\n    Extract activations from all layers of the base model.\n    Returns shape: (n_layers, n_samples, hidden_dim)\n    \"\"\"\n    base_model.eval()\n    device = next(base_model.parameters()).device\n\n    all_layer_activations = None\n    n_layers = None\n\n    for i in range(0, len(texts), batch_size):\n        batch_texts = texts[i:i + batch_size]\n\n        with torch.no_grad():\n            inputs = tokenizer(\n                batch_texts,\n                return_tensors=\"pt\",\n                truncation=True,\n                max_length=512,\n                padding=True\n            )\n            inputs = {k: v.to(device) for k, v in inputs.items()}\n            attention_mask = inputs.get('attention_mask', None)\n\n            outputs = base_model(**inputs, output_hidden_states=True)\n            hidden_states = outputs.hidden_states  # Tuple of (batch, seq_len, hidden_dim)\n\n            if n_layers is None:\n                n_layers = len(hidden_states)\n                all_layer_activations = [[] for _ in range(n_layers)]\n\n            for layer_idx in range(n_layers):\n                hs = hidden_states[layer_idx].cpu().float().numpy()  # (batch, seq_len, hidden_dim)\n\n                if aggregation == 'first':\n                    act = hs[:, 0, :]\n                elif aggregation == 'last':\n                    # Use last non-padded token\n                    if attention_mask is not None:\n                        mask = attention_mask.cpu().numpy()\n                        batch_act = []\n                        for b in range(hs.shape[0]):\n                            last_idx = int(mask[b].sum()) - 1\n                            batch_act.append(hs[b, last_idx, :])\n                        act = np.array(batch_act)\n                    else:\n                        act = hs[:, -1, :]\n                elif aggregation == 'mean':\n                    if attention_mask is not None:\n                        mask = attention_mask.cpu().numpy()[:, :, None]  # (batch, seq_len, 1)\n                        masked_hs = hs * mask\n                        act = masked_hs.sum(axis=1) / mask.sum(axis=1)\n                    else:\n                        act = hs.mean(axis=1)\n                elif aggregation == 'max':\n                    if attention_mask is not None:\n                        mask = attention_mask.cpu().numpy()[:, :, None]\n                        masked_hs = hs * mask + (1 - mask) * (-1e9)\n                        act = masked_hs.max(axis=1)\n                    else:\n                        act = hs.max(axis=1)\n                else:\n                    raise ValueError(f\"Unknown aggregation: {aggregation}\")\n\n                all_layer_activations[layer_idx].append(act)\n\n        if (i // batch_size) % 10 == 0:\n            print(f\"  Processed {min(i + batch_size, len(texts))}/{len(texts)} texts\")\n\n    # Concatenate batches for each layer\n    result = []\n    for layer_idx in range(n_layers):\n        result.append(np.concatenate(all_layer_activations[layer_idx], axis=0))\n\n    return np.array(result), n_layers\n\n\ndef train_and_evaluate_probe(X, y, cv_folds=5, max_iter=2000):\n    \"\"\"Train a logistic regression probe with cross-validation.\"\"\"\n    scaler = StandardScaler()\n    X_scaled = scaler.fit_transform(X)\n\n    probe = LogisticRegression(max_iter=max_iter, random_state=42, C=1.0, solver='lbfgs')\n\n    skf = StratifiedKFold(n_splits=cv_folds, shuffle=True, random_state=42)\n\n    cv_accuracies = []\n    cv_f1s = []\n    cv_aucs = []\n\n    for train_idx, val_idx in skf.split(X_scaled, y):\n        X_train, X_val = X_scaled[train_idx], X_scaled[val_idx]\n        y_train, y_val = y[train_idx], y[val_idx]\n\n        probe_cv = LogisticRegression(max_iter=max_iter, random_state=42, C=1.0, solver='lbfgs')\n        probe_cv.fit(X_train, y_train)\n\n        y_pred = probe_cv.predict(X_val)\n        y_proba = probe_cv.predict_proba(X_val)[:, 1]\n\n        cv_accuracies.append(accuracy_score(y_val, y_pred))\n        _, _, f1, _ = precision_recall_fscore_support(y_val, y_pred, average='binary', zero_division=0)\n        cv_f1s.append(f1)\n        try:\n            cv_aucs.append(roc_auc_score(y_val, y_proba))\n        except ValueError:\n            cv_aucs.append(0.5)\n\n    # Train final probe on all data\n    probe.fit(X_scaled, y)\n\n    return {\n        'probe': probe,\n        'scaler': scaler,\n        'cv_accuracy_mean': np.mean(cv_accuracies),\n        'cv_accuracy_std': np.std(cv_accuracies),\n        'cv_f1_mean': np.mean(cv_f1s),\n        'cv_f1_std': np.std(cv_f1s),\n        'cv_auc_mean': np.mean(cv_aucs),\n        'cv_auc_std': np.std(cv_aucs),\n        'cv_accuracies': cv_accuracies,\n        'cv_f1s': cv_f1s,\n        'cv_aucs': cv_aucs,\n    }\n\n\ndef main():\n    start_time = time.time()\n\n    # ==========================================\n    # Load data\n    # ==========================================\n    print(\"Loading data...\")\n    data = load_data()\n    texts = [item['text'] for item in data]\n    print(f\"Loaded {len(data)} examples\")\n\n    # ==========================================\n    # Step 1: Generate behavioral labels\n    # ==========================================\n    print(\"\\nLoading causal LM model for generation...\")\n    tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained(MODEL_NAME, trust_remote_code=True)\n    if tokenizer.pad_token is None:\n        tokenizer.pad_token = tokenizer.eos_token\n\n    gen_model = AutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained(\n        MODEL_NAME,\n        torch_dtype=torch.float16,\n        trust_remote_code=True\n    ).cuda()\n\n    labels = generate_behavioral_labels(data, tokenizer, gen_model)\n    save_behavioral_labels(data, labels)\n    labels = np.array(labels)\n\n    print(f\"\\nLabel distribution: {np.sum(labels == 1)} correct, {np.sum(labels == 0)} incorrect\")\n\n    # Free generation model memory\n    del gen_model\n    torch.cuda.empty_cache()\n\n    elapsed = time.time() - start_time\n    print(f\"\\nStep 1 complete. Time elapsed: {elapsed/60:.1f} minutes\")\n\n    # ==========================================\n    # Step 2: Extract activations from base model\n    # ==========================================\n    print(\"\\n\" + \"=\" * 60)\n    print(\"STEP 2: Extracting activations from all layers\")\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n\n    print(\"Loading base model for activation extraction...\")\n    base_model = AutoModel.from_pretrained(\n        MODEL_NAME,\n        torch_dtype=torch.float16,\n        trust_remote_code=True\n    ).cuda()\n\n    # Test aggregation strategies\n    aggregation_methods = ['mean', 'last', 'first', 'max']\n    all_results = {}  # {aggregation: {layer: probe_result}}\n\n    for agg_method in aggregation_methods:\n        print(f\"\\n--- Extracting activations with aggregation='{agg_method}' ---\")\n        activations, n_layers = extract_activations_all_layers(\n            base_model, tokenizer, texts,\n            aggregation=agg_method,\n            batch_size=16\n        )\n        print(f\"Activations shape: {activations.shape} (n_layers={n_layers})\")\n\n        # ==========================================\n        # Step 3: Train probes for all layers\n        # ==========================================\n        print(f\"\\n--- Training probes for all {n_layers} layers (agg='{agg_method}') ---\")\n        layer_results = {}\n\n        for layer_idx in range(n_layers):\n            X = activations[layer_idx]\n            result = train_and_evaluate_probe(X, labels)\n            result['layer'] = layer_idx\n            result['aggregation'] = agg_method\n            layer_results[layer_idx] = result\n\n            if layer_idx % 4 == 0 or layer_idx == n_layers - 1:\n                print(f\"  Layer {layer_idx:2d}: CV Acc={result['cv_accuracy_mean']:.3f}±{result['cv_accuracy_std']:.3f}, \"\n                      f\"F1={result['cv_f1_mean']:.3f}±{result['cv_f1_std']:.3f}, \"\n                      f\"AUC={result['cv_auc_mean']:.3f}±{result['cv_auc_std']:.3f}\")\n\n        all_results[agg_method] = layer_results\n\n        elapsed = time.time() - start_time\n        print(f\"\\nAggregation '{agg_method}' complete. Time elapsed: {elapsed/60:.1f} minutes\")\n\n    # Free base model\n    del base_model\n    del activations\n    torch.cuda.empty_cache()\n\n    # ==========================================\n    # Step 4: Find best probe\n    # ==========================================\n    print(\"\\n\" + \"=\" * 60)\n    print(\"STEP 4: Finding best probe configuration\")\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n\n    best_config = None\n    best_auc = -1\n\n    for agg_method, layer_results in all_results.items():\n        for layer_idx, result in layer_results.items():\n            if result['cv_auc_mean'] > best_auc:\n                best_auc = result['cv_auc_mean']\n                best_config = (agg_method, layer_idx, result)\n\n    best_agg, best_layer, best_result = best_config\n    print(f\"\\nBest configuration:\")\n    print(f\"  Aggregation: {best_agg}\")\n    print(f\"  Layer: {best_layer}\")\n    print(f\"  CV Accuracy: {best_result['cv_accuracy_mean']:.4f} ± {best_result['cv_accuracy_std']:.4f}\")\n    print(f\"  CV F1: {best_result['cv_f1_mean']:.4f} ± {best_result['cv_f1_std']:.4f}\")\n    print(f\"  CV AUC: {best_result['cv_auc_mean']:.4f} ± {best_result['cv_auc_std']:.4f}\")\n\n    # ==========================================\n    # Save best probe\n    # ==========================================\n    probe_save_data = {\n        'model': best_result['probe'],\n        'scaler': best_result['scaler'],\n        'layer': best_layer,\n        'aggregation': best_agg,\n        'cv_accuracy_mean': best_result['cv_accuracy_mean'],\n        'cv_f1_mean': best_result['cv_f1_mean'],\n        'cv_auc_mean': best_result['cv_auc_mean'],\n    }\n\n    probe_path = FINAL_PROBE_DIR / \"probe.pkl\"\n    with open(probe_path, 'wb') as f:\n        pickle.dump(probe_save_data, f)\n    print(f\"Saved best probe to {probe_path}\")\n\n    # ==========================================\n    # Step 5: Generate metrics and visualizations\n    # ==========================================\n    print(\"\\n\" + \"=\" * 60)\n    print(\"STEP 5: Generating metrics and visualizations\")\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n\n    # Compile metrics\n    metrics = {\n        'best_layer': int(best_layer),\n        'best_aggregation': best_agg,\n        'best_cv_accuracy': float(best_result['cv_accuracy_mean']),\n        'best_cv_accuracy_std': float(best_result['cv_accuracy_std']),\n        'best_cv_f1': float(best_result['cv_f1_mean']),\n        'best_cv_f1_std': float(best_result['cv_f1_std']),\n        'best_cv_auc': float(best_result['cv_auc_mean']),\n        'best_cv_auc_std': float(best_result['cv_auc_std']),\n        'label_distribution': {\n            'correct': int(np.sum(labels == 1)),\n            'incorrect': int(np.sum(labels == 0)),\n            'total': int(len(labels))\n        },\n        'all_layer_results': {}\n    }\n\n    for agg_method, layer_results in all_results.items():\n        metrics['all_layer_results'][agg_method] = {}\n        for layer_idx, result in layer_results.items():\n            metrics['all_layer_results'][agg_method][str(layer_idx)] = {\n                'cv_accuracy_mean': float(result['cv_accuracy_mean']),\n                'cv_accuracy_std': float(result['cv_accuracy_std']),\n                'cv_f1_mean': float(result['cv_f1_mean']),\n                'cv_f1_std': float(result['cv_f1_std']),\n                'cv_auc_mean': float(result['cv_auc_mean']),\n                'cv_auc_std': float(result['cv_auc_std']),\n            }\n\n    with open(METRICS_FILE, 'w') as f:\n        json.dump(metrics, f, indent=2)\n    print(f\"Saved metrics to {METRICS_FILE}\")\n\n    # ==========================================\n    # Visualization 1: sys\nimport time\nimport re\nimport numpy as np\nimport torch\nfrom pathlib import Path\nfrom transformers import AutoModelForCausalLM, AutoTokenizer, AutoModel\nfrom sklearn.linear_model import LogisticRegression\nfrom sklearn.model_selection import cross_val_score, StratifiedKFold\nfrom sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler\nfrom sklearn.metrics import (\n    accuracy_score, precision_recall_fscore_support,\n    roc_auc_score, classification_report, roc_curve\n)\nimport matplotlib\nmatplotlib.use('Agg')\nimport matplotlib.pyplot as plt\n\nWORK_DIR = Path(\"/iopsstor/scratch/cscs/oyasunaga/autointerp_runs/jobs/truth_analysis_Qwen_Qwen2.5-1.5B_2513489\")\nMODEL_NAME = \"Qwen/Qwen2.5-1.5B\"\nDATA_FILE = WORK_DIR / \"labeled_data.jsonl\"\nBEHAVIORAL_LABELS_FILE = WORK_DIR / \"behavioral_labels.jsonl\"\nFINAL_PROBE_DIR = WORK_DIR / \"final_probe\"\nMETRICS_FILE = WORK_DIR / \"metrics.json\"\n\nos.makedirs(FINAL_PROBE_DIR, exist_ok=True)\n\n\ndef load_data():\n    \"\"\"Load labeled data from jsonl.\"\"\"\n    data = []\n    with open(DATA_FILE, 'r') as f:\n        for line in f:\n            data.append(json.loads(line))\n    return data\n\n\ndef normalize_text(text):\n    \"\"\"Normalize text for comparison.\"\"\"\n    text = text.lower().strip()\n    # Remove punctuation at end\n    text = re.sub(r'[.,;:!?\\s]+$', '', text)\n    # Remove articles at start\n    text = re.sub(r'^(the|a|an)\\s+', '', text)\n    return text\n\n\ndef check_answer_correctness(model_response, correct_answers):\n    \"\"\"\n    Check if the model's response matches any correct answer.\n    Uses flexible matching: checks if any correct answer is contained\n    in the model response or vice versa.\n    \"\"\"\n    response_lower = model_response.lower().strip()\n    response_normalized = normalize_text(response_lower)\n\n    for correct in correct_answers:\n        correct_lower = correct.lower().strip()\n        correct_normalized = normalize_text(correct_lower)\n\n        # Direct containment check\n        if correct_normalized in response_normalized:\n            return True\n        if response_normalized in correct_normalized:\n            return True\n\n        # Check key phrases (extract important words)\n        # Split correct answer into significant words (>3 chars)\n        key_words = [w for w in correct_normalized.split() if len(w) > 3]\n        if len(key_words) >= 2:\n            matches = sum(1 for w in key_words if w in response_normalized)\n            if matches >= len(key_words) * 0.6:\n                return True\n\n    return False\n\n\ndef generate_behavioral_labels(data, tokenizer, model):\n    \"\"\"\n    Generate behavioral labels by running the model on each question.\n    label=1 if model answers correctly, label=0 if incorrect.\n    \"\"\"\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n    print(\"STEP 1: Generating behavioral labels\")\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n\n    model.eval()\n    labels = []\n    correct_count = 0\n\n    for i, item in enumerate(data):\n        question = item['text']\n        correct_answers = item['correct_answers']\n\n        # Format as a simple Q&A prompt\n        prompt = f\"Q: {question}\\nA:\"\n\n        inputs = tokenizer(prompt, return_tensors=\"pt\", truncation=True, max_length=256)\n        inputs = {k: v.cuda() for k, v in inputs.items()}\n\n        with torch.no_grad():\n            outputs = model.generate(\n                **inputs,\n                max_new_tokens=100,\n                do_sample=False,\n                temperature=1.0,\n                pad_token_id=tokenizer.eos_token_id,\n            )\n\n        # Decode only the generated part\n        input_len = inputs['input_ids'].shape[1]\n        generated = tokenizer.decode(outputs[0][input_len:], skip_special_tokens=True).strip()\n\n        # Check correctness\n        is_correct = check_answer_correctness(generated, correct_answers)\n        label = 1 if is_correct else 0\n        labels.append(label)\n\n        if is_correct:\n            correct_count += 1\n\n        if i < 10 or (i < 100 and i % 20 == 0) or i % 100 == 0:\n            print(f\"\\n[{i}/{len(data)}] Q: {question[:80]}...\")\n            print(f\"  Generated: {generated[:120]}...\")\n            print(f\"  Correct answers: {correct_answers[0][:80]}...\")\n            print(f\"  Label: {label} ({'correct' if label else 'incorrect'})\")\n\n    print(f\"\\n{'=' * 40}\")\n    print(f\"Total correct: {correct_count}/{len(data)} ({correct_count/len(data)*100:.1f}%)\")\n    print(f\"Total incorrect: {len(data) - correct_count}/{len(data)} ({(len(data)-correct_count)/len(data)*100:.1f}%)\")\n\n    return labels\n\n\ndef save_behavioral_labels(data, labels):\n    \"\"\"Save behavioral labels to jsonl.\"\"\"\n    with open(BEHAVIORAL_LABELS_FILE, 'w') as f:\n        for item, label in zip(data, labels):\n            entry = {\"text\": item['text'], \"label\": label}\n            f.write(json.dumps(entry) + '\\n')\n    print(f\"Saved behavioral labels to {BEHAVIORAL_LABELS_FILE}\")\n\n\ndef extract_activations_all_layers(base_model, tokenizer, texts, aggregation='mean', batch_size=16):\n    \"\"\"\n    Extract activations from all layers of the base model.\n    Returns shape: (n_layers, n_samples, hidden_dim)\n    \"\"\"\n    base_model.eval()\n    device = next(base_model.parameters()).device\n\n    all_layer_activations = None\n    n_layers = None\n\n    for i in range(0, len(texts), batch_size):\n        batch_texts = texts[i:i + batch_size]\n\n        with torch.no_grad():\n            inputs = tokenizer(\n                batch_texts,\n                return_tensors=\"pt\",\n                truncation=True,\n                max_length=512,\n                padding=True\n            )\n            inputs = {k: v.to(device) for k, v in inputs.items()}\n            attention_mask = inputs.get('attention_mask', None)\n\n            outputs = base_model(**inputs, output_hidden_states=True)\n            hidden_states = outputs.hidden_states  # Tuple of (batch, seq_len, hidden_dim)\n\n            if n_layers is None:\n                n_layers = len(hidden_states)\n                all_layer_activations = [[] for _ in range(n_layers)]\n\n            for layer_idx in range(n_layers):\n                hs = hidden_states[layer_idx].cpu().float().numpy()  # (batch, seq_len, hidden_dim)\n\n                if aggregation == 'first':\n                    act = hs[:, 0, :]\n                elif aggregation == 'last':\n                    # Use last non-padded token\n                    if attention_mask is not None:\n                        mask = attention_mask.cpu().numpy()\n                        batch_act = []\n                        for b in range(hs.shape[0]):\n                            last_idx = int(mask[b].sum()) - 1\n                            batch_act.append(hs[b, last_idx, :])\n                        act = np.array(batch_act)\n                    else:\n                        act = hs[:, -1, :]\n                elif aggregation == 'mean':\n                    if attention_mask is not None:\n                        mask = attention_mask.cpu().numpy()[:, :, None]  # (batch, seq_len, 1)\n                        masked_hs = hs * mask\n                        act = masked_hs.sum(axis=1) / mask.sum(axis=1)\n                    else:\n                        act = hs.mean(axis=1)\n                elif aggregation == 'max':\n                    if attention_mask is not None:\n                        mask = attention_mask.cpu().numpy()[:, :, None]\n                        masked_hs = hs * mask + (1 - mask) * (-1e9)\n                        act = masked_hs.max(axis=1)\n                    else:\n                        act = hs.max(axis=1)\n                else:\n                    raise ValueError(f\"Unknown aggregation: {aggregation}\")\n\n                all_layer_activations[layer_idx].append(act)\n\n        if (i // batch_size) % 10 == 0:\n            print(f\"  Processed {min(i + batch_size, len(texts))}/{len(texts)} texts\")\n\n    # Concatenate batches for each layer\n    result = []\n    for layer_idx in range(n_layers):\n        result.append(np.concatenate(all_layer_activations[layer_idx], axis=0))\n\n    return np.array(result), n_layers\n\n\ndef train_and_evaluate_probe(X, y, cv_folds=5, max_iter=2000):\n    \"\"\"Train a logistic regression probe with cross-validation.\"\"\"\n    scaler = StandardScaler()\n    X_scaled = scaler.fit_transform(X)\n\n    probe = LogisticRegression(max_iter=max_iter, random_state=42, C=1.0, solver='lbfgs')\n\n    skf = StratifiedKFold(n_splits=cv_folds, shuffle=True, random_state=42)\n\n    cv_accuracies = []\n    cv_f1s = []\n    cv_aucs = []\n\n    for train_idx, val_idx in skf.split(X_scaled, y):\n        X_train, X_val = X_scaled[train_idx], X_scaled[val_idx]\n        y_train, y_val = y[train_idx], y[val_idx]\n\n        probe_cv = LogisticRegression(max_iter=max_iter, random_state=42, C=1.0, solver='lbfgs')\n        probe_cv.fit(X_train, y_train)\n\n        y_pred = probe_cv.predict(X_val)\n        y_proba = probe_cv.predict_proba(X_val)[:, 1]\n\n        cv_accuracies.append(accuracy_score(y_val, y_pred))\n        _, _, f1, _ = precision_recall_fscore_support(y_val, y_pred, average='binary', zero_division=0)\n        cv_f1s.append(f1)\n        try:\n            cv_aucs.append(roc_auc_score(y_val, y_proba))\n        except ValueError:\n            cv_aucs.append(0.5)\n\n    # Train final probe on all data\n    probe.fit(X_scaled, y)\n\n    return {\n        'probe': probe,\n        'scaler': scaler,\n        'cv_accuracy_mean': np.mean(cv_accuracies),\n        'cv_accuracy_std': np.std(cv_accuracies),\n        'cv_f1_mean': np.mean(cv_f1s),\n        'cv_f1_std': np.std(cv_f1s),\n        'cv_auc_mean': np.mean(cv_aucs),\n        'cv_auc_std': np.std(cv_aucs),\n        'cv_accuracies': cv_accuracies,\n        'cv_f1s': cv_f1s,\n        'cv_aucs': cv_aucs,\n    }\n\n\ndef main():\n    start_time = time.time()\n\n    # ==========================================\n    # Load data\n    # ==========================================\n    print(\"Loading data...\")\n    data = load_data()\n    texts = [item['text'] for item in data]\n    print(f\"Loaded {len(data)} examples\")\n\n    # ==========================================\n    # Step 1: Generate behavioral labels\n    # ==========================================\n    print(\"\\nLoading causal LM model for generation...\")\n    tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained(MODEL_NAME, trust_remote_code=True)\n    if tokenizer.pad_token is None:\n        tokenizer.pad_token = tokenizer.eos_token\n\n    gen_model = AutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained(\n        MODEL_NAME,\n        torch_dtype=torch.float16,\n        trust_remote_code=True\n    ).cuda()\n\n    labels = generate_behavioral_labels(data, tokenizer, gen_model)\n    save_behavioral_labels(data, labels)\n    labels = np.array(labels)\n\n    print(f\"\\nLabel distribution: {np.sum(labels == 1)} correct, {np.sum(labels == 0)} incorrect\")\n\n    # Free generation model memory\n    del gen_model\n    torch.cuda.empty_cache()\n\n    elapsed = time.time() - start_time\n    print(f\"\\nStep 1 complete. Time elapsed: {elapsed/60:.1f} minutes\")\n\n    # ==========================================\n    # Step 2: Extract activations from base model\n    # ==========================================\n    print(\"\\n\" + \"=\" * 60)\n    print(\"STEP 2: Extracting activations from all layers\")\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n\n    print(\"Loading base model for activation extraction...\")\n    base_model = AutoModel.from_pretrained(\n        MODEL_NAME,\n        torch_dtype=torch.float16,\n        trust_remote_code=True\n    ).cuda()\n\n    # Test aggregation strategies\n    aggregation_methods = ['mean', 'last', 'first', 'max']\n    all_results = {}  # {aggregation: {layer: probe_result}}\n\n    for agg_method in aggregation_methods:\n        print(f\"\\n--- Extracting activations with aggregation='{agg_method}' ---\")\n        activations, n_layers = extract_activations_all_layers(\n            base_model, tokenizer, texts,\n            aggregation=agg_method,\n            batch_size=16\n        )\n        print(f\"Activations shape: {activations.shape} (n_layers={n_layers})\")\n\n        # ==========================================\n        # Step 3: Train probes for all layers\n        # ==========================================\n        print(f\"\\n--- Training probes for all {n_layers} layers (agg='{agg_method}') ---\")\n        layer_results = {}\n\n        for layer_idx in range(n_layers):\n            X = activations[layer_idx]\n            result = train_and_evaluate_probe(X, labels)\n            result['layer'] = layer_idx\n            result['aggregation'] = agg_method\n            layer_results[layer_idx] = result\n\n            if layer_idx % 4 == 0 or layer_idx == n_layers - 1:\n                print(f\"  Layer {layer_idx:2d}: CV Acc={result['cv_accuracy_mean']:.3f}±{result['cv_accuracy_std']:.3f}, \"\n                      f\"F1={result['cv_f1_mean']:.3f}±{result['cv_f1_std']:.3f}, \"\n                      f\"AUC={result['cv_auc_mean']:.3f}±{result['cv_auc_std']:.3f}\")\n\n        all_results[agg_method] = layer_results\n\n        elapsed = time.time() - start_time\n        print(f\"\\nAggregation '{agg_method}' complete. Time elapsed: {elapsed/60:.1f} minutes\")\n\n    # Free base model\n    del base_model\n    del activations\n    torch.cuda.empty_cache()\n\n    # ==========================================\n    # Step 4: Find best probe\n    # ==========================================\n    print(\"\\n\" + \"=\" * 60)\n    print(\"STEP 4: Finding best probe configuration\")\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n\n    best_config = None\n    best_auc = -1\n\n    for agg_method, layer_results in all_results.items():\n        for layer_idx, result in layer_results.items():\n            if result['cv_auc_mean'] > python3\n\"\"\"\nComplete pipeline for truth analysis probing on Qwen2.5-1.5B.\nStep 1: Generate behavioral labels by running model on TruthfulQA questions.\nStep 2: Extract activations from all layers.\nStep 3: Train linear probes across layers and token aggregation strategies.\nStep 4: Evaluate, visualize, and save best probe.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport json\nimport os\nimport pickle\nimport sys\nimport time\nimport re\nimport numpy as np\nimport torch\nfrom pathlib import Path\nfrom transformers import AutoModelForCausalLM, AutoTokenizer, AutoModel\nfrom sklearn.linear_model import LogisticRegression\nfrom sklearn.model_selection import cross_val_score, StratifiedKFold\nfrom sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler\nfrom sklearn.metrics import (\n    accuracy_score, precision_recall_fscore_support,\n    roc_auc_score, classification_report, roc_curve\n)\nimport matplotlib\nmatplotlib.use('Agg')\nimport matplotlib.pyplot as plt\n\nWORK_DIR = Path(\"/iopsstor/scratch/cscs/oyasunaga/autointerp_runs/jobs/truth_analysis_Qwen_Qwen2.5-1.5B_2513489\")\nMODEL_NAME = \"Qwen/Qwen2.5-1.5B\"\nDATA_FILE = WORK_DIR / \"labeled_data.jsonl\"\nBEHAVIORAL_LABELS_FILE = WORK_DIR / \"behavioral_labels.jsonl\"\nFINAL_PROBE_DIR = WORK_DIR / \"final_probe\"\nMETRICS_FILE = WORK_DIR / \"metrics.json\"\n\nos.makedirs(FINAL_PROBE_DIR, exist_ok=True)\n\n\ndef load_data():\n    \"\"\"Load labeled data from jsonl.\"\"\"\n    data = []\n    with open(DATA_FILE, 'r') as f:\n        for line in f:\n            data.append(json.loads(line))\n    return data\n\n\ndef get_yes_no_stance(text):\n    \"\"\"\n    Determine if text has a clear yes/no stance.\n    Returns 'yes', 'no', or None.\n    \"\"\"\n    text_lower = text.lower().strip()\n    # Check first word/phrase\n    first_part = text_lower[:50]\n\n    # Strong yes indicators\n    if re.match(r'^(yes|yeah|yep|correct|absolutely|indeed|of course|sure|definitely|certainly|right)\\b', first_part):\n        return 'yes'\n\n    # Strong no indicators\n    if re.match(r'^(no|nope|not|nah|incorrect|wrong|neither|none|never)\\b', first_part):\n        return 'no'\n\n    # Check for \"X is not\" or \"X does not\" patterns\n    if re.search(r'\\b(is not|isn\\'t|are not|aren\\'t|does not|doesn\\'t|do not|don\\'t|cannot|can\\'t|has not|hasn\\'t|have not|haven\\'t|was not|wasn\\'t|were not|weren\\'t)\\b', first_part):\n        return 'no'\n\n    return None\n\n\ndef check_answer_correctness(model_response, correct_answers, question):\n    \"\"\"\n    Check if the model's response matches any correct answer.\n    Uses multiple strategies:\n    1. Yes/No direction matching for yes/no questions\n    2. Key entity/fact matching\n    3. Semantic content matching\n    \"\"\"\n    response_lower = model_response.lower().strip()\n    # Truncate response to first meaningful sentence\n    # Many responses go on tangents after the first sentence\n    first_sentence = response_lower.split('\\n')[0].strip()\n    if len(first_sentence) < 5:\n        first_sentence = response_lower[:200]\n\n    # Strategy 1: Yes/No direction matching\n    response_stance = get_yes_no_stance(first_sentence)\n    if response_stance is not None:\n        for correct in correct_answers:\n            correct_stance = get_yes_no_stance(correct.lower())\n            if correct_stance is not None:\n                # Both have a stance - check if they match\n                if response_stance == correct_stance:\n                    return True\n                else:\n                    return False\n\n    # Strategy 2: Check for key factual content\n    # Extract key content words from correct answers (removing common words)\n    stop_words = {'the', 'a', 'an', 'is', 'are', 'was', 'were', 'be', 'been', 'being',\n                  'have', 'has', 'had', 'do', 'does', 'did', 'will', 'would', 'could',\n                  'should', 'may', 'might', 'can', 'shall', 'must', 'need', 'dare',\n                  'to', 'of', 'in', 'for', 'on', 'with', 'at', 'by', 'from', 'as',\n                  'into', 'through', 'during', 'before', 'after', 'above', 'below',\n                  'between', 'out', 'off', 'over', 'under', 'again', 'further',\n                  'then', 'once', 'and', 'but', 'or', 'nor', 'not', 'so', 'yet',\n                  'both', 'each', 'few', 'more', 'most', 'other', 'some', 'such',\n                  'only', 'own', 'same', 'than', 'too', 'very', 'just', 'because',\n                  'that', 'this', 'these', 'those', 'it', 'its', 'they', 'them',\n                  'their', 'we', 'our', 'you', 'your', 'he', 'she', 'him', 'her',\n                  'his', 'who', 'which', 'what', 'when', 'where', 'how', 'why',\n                  'all', 'any', 'no', 'yes', 'if', 'about', 'up', 'there', 'here',\n                  'also', 'said', 'says', 'say'}\n\n    best_match_score = 0\n\n    for correct in correct_answers:\n        correct_lower = correct.lower().strip()\n\n        # Direct substring matching (relaxed)\n        # Remove common phrases from correct answer\n        correct_core = re.sub(r'^(yes|no|no,|yes,)\\s*', '', correct_lower).strip()\n\n        if correct_core in first_sentence or first_sentence in correct_core:\n            return True\n\n        # Key word matching\n        correct_words = set(re.findall(r'\\b[a-z]+\\b', correct_lower)) - stop_words\n        response_words = set(re.findall(r'\\b[a-z]+\\b', first_sentence)) - stop_words\n\n        if len(correct_words) > 0:\n            # Check overlap of correct words found in response\n            overlap = correct_words & response_words\n            score = len(overlap) / len(correct_words)\n            best_match_score = max(best_match_score, score)\n\n    # Strategy 3: Check for \"I have no comment\" or uncertainty markers (often correct for TruthfulQA)\n    uncertainty_markers = ['i have no comment', 'i don\\'t know', 'i\\'m not sure',\n                           'it\\'s unclear', 'there is no evidence', 'uncertain',\n                           'it depends', 'cannot be determined']\n    for marker in uncertainty_markers:\n        if marker in first_sentence:\n            for correct in correct_answers:\n                if any(um in correct.lower() for um in ['no comment', 'uncertain', 'unclear', 'ambiguous']):\n                    return True\n\n    # Threshold for key word matching\n    if best_match_score >= 0.5:\n        return True\n\n    return False\n\n\ndef generate_behavioral_labels(data, tokenizer, model):\n    \"\"\"\n    Generate behavioral labels by running the model on each question.\n    label=1 if model answers correctly, label=0 if incorrect.\n    \"\"\"\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n    print(\"STEP 1: Generating behavioral labels\")\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n\n    model.eval()\n    labels = []\n    correct_count = 0\n    responses = []\n\n    for i, item in enumerate(data):\n        question = item['text']\n        correct_answers = item['correct_answers']\n\n        # Format as a simple Q&A prompt\n        prompt = f\"Q: {question}\\nA:\"\n\n        inputs = tokenizer(prompt, return_tensors=\"pt\", truncation=True, max_length=256)\n        inputs = {k: v.cuda() for k, v in inputs.items()}\n\n        with torch.no_grad():\n            outputs = model.generate(\n                **inputs,\n                max_new_tokens=80,\n                do_sample=False,\n                temperature=1.0,\n                pad_token_id=tokenizer.eos_token_id,\n            )\n\n        # Decode only the generated part\n        input_len = inputs['input_ids'].shape[1]\n        generated = tokenizer.decode(outputs[0][input_len:], skip_special_tokens=True).strip()\n\n        # Check correctness\n        is_correct = check_answer_correctness(generated, correct_answers, question)\n        label = 1 if is_correct else 0\n        labels.append(label)\n        responses.append(generated)\n\n        if is_correct:\n            correct_count += 1\n\n        if i < 15 or (i < 100 and i % 25 == 0) or i % 100 == 0:\n            print(f\"\\n[{i}/{len(data)}] Q: {question[:80]}...\")\n            print(f\"  Generated: {generated[:120]}...\")\n            print(f\"  Correct answers: {correct_answers[0][:80]}...\")\n            print(f\"  Label: {label} ({'correct' if label else 'incorrect'})\")\n\n    print(f\"\\n{'=' * 40}\")\n    print(f\"Total correct: {correct_count}/{len(data)} ({correct_count/len(data)*100:.1f}%)\")\n    print(f\"Total incorrect: {len(data) - correct_count}/{len(data)} ({(len(data)-correct_count)/len(data)*100:.1f}%)\")\n\n    return labels, responses\n\n\ndef save_behavioral_labels(data, labels):\n    \"\"\"Save behavioral labels to jsonl.\"\"\"\n    with open(BEHAVIORAL_LABELS_FILE, 'w') as f:\n        for item, label in zip(data, labels):\n            entry = {\"text\": item['text'], \"label\": label}\n            f.write(json.dumps(entry) + '\\n')\n    print(f\"Saved behavioral labels to {BEHAVIORAL_LABELS_FILE}\")\n\n\ndef extract_activations_all_layers(base_model, tokenizer, texts, aggregation='mean', batch_size=16):\n    \"\"\"\n    Extract activations from all layers of the base model.\n    Returns shape: (n_layers, n_samples, hidden_dim)\n    \"\"\"\n    base_model.eval()\n    device = next(base_model.parameters()).device\n\n    all_layer_activations = None\n    n_layers = None\n\n    for i in range(0, len(texts), batch_size):\n        batch_texts = texts[i:i + batch_size]\n\n        with torch.no_grad():\n            inputs = tokenizer(\n                batch_texts,\n                return_tensors=\"pt\",\n                truncation=True,\n                max_length=512,\n                padding=True\n            )\n            inputs = {k: v.to(device) for k, v in inputs.items()}\n            attention_mask = inputs.get('attention_mask', None)\n\n            outputs = base_model(**inputs, output_hidden_states=True)\n            hidden_states = outputs.hidden_states  # Tuple of (batch, seq_len, hidden_dim)\n\n            if n_layers is None:\n                n_layers = len(hidden_states)\n                all_layer_activations = [[] for _ in range(n_layers)]\n\n            for layer_idx in range(n_layers):\n                hs = hidden_states[layer_idx].cpu().float().numpy()  # (batch, seq_len, hidden_dim)\n\n                if aggregation == 'first':\n                    act = hs[:, 0, :]\n                elif aggregation == 'last':\n                    # Use last non-padded token\n                    if attention_mask is not None:\n                        mask = attention_mask.cpu().numpy()\n                        batch_act = []\n                        for b in range(hs.shape[0]):\n                            last_idx = int(mask[b].sum()) - 1\n                            batch_act.append(hs[b, last_idx, :])\n                        act = np.array(batch_act)\n                    else:\n                        act = hs[:, -1, :]\n                elif aggregation == 'mean':\n                    if attention_mask is not None:\n                        mask = attention_mask.cpu().numpy()[:, :, None]  # (batch, seq_len, 1)\n                        masked_hs = hs * mask\n                        act = masked_hs.sum(axis=1) / np.maximum(mask.sum(axis=1), 1e-8)\n                    else:\n                        act = hs.mean(axis=1)\n                elif aggregation == 'max':\n                    if attention_mask is not None:\n                        mask = attention_mask.cpu().numpy()[:, :, None]\n                        masked_hs = hs * mask + (1 - mask) * (-1e9)\n                        act = masked_hs.max(axis=1)\n                    else:\n                        act = hs.max(axis=1)\n                else:\n                    raise ValueError(f\"Unknown aggregation: {aggregation}\")\n\n                all_layer_activations[layer_idx].append(act)\n\n        if (i // batch_size) % 10 == 0:\n            print(f\"  Processed {min(i + batch_size, len(texts))}/{len(texts)} texts\")\n\n    # Concatenate batches for each layer\n    result = []\n    for layer_idx in range(n_layers):\n        result.append(np.concatenate(all_layer_activations[layer_idx], axis=0))\n\n    return np.array(result), n_layers\n\n\ndef train_and_evaluate_probe(X, y, cv_folds=5, max_iter=2000):\n    \"\"\"Train a logistic regression probe with cross-validation.\"\"\"\n    scaler = StandardScaler()\n    X_scaled = scaler.fit_transform(X)\n\n    probe = LogisticRegression(max_iter=max_iter, random_state=42, C=1.0, solver='lbfgs')\n\n    skf = StratifiedKFold(n_splits=cv_folds, shuffle=True, random_state=42)\n\n    cv_accuracies = []\n    cv_f1s = []\n    cv_aucs = []\n    cv_precisions = []\n    cv_recalls = []\n\n    for train_idx, val_idx in skf.split(X_scaled, y):\n        X_train, X_val = X_scaled[train_idx], X_scaled[val_idx]\n        y_train, y_val = y[train_idx], y[val_idx]\n\n        probe_cv = LogisticRegression(max_iter=max_iter, random_state=42, C=1.0, solver='lbfgs')\n        probe_cv.fit(X_train, y_train)\n\n        y_pred = probe_cv.predict(X_val)\n        y_proba = probe_cv.predict_proba(X_val)[:, 1]\n\n        cv_accuracies.append(accuracy_score(y_val, y_pred))\n        prec, rec, f1, _ = precision_recall_fscore_support(y_val, y_pred, average='binary', zero_division=0)\n        cv_f1s.append(f1)\n        cv_precisions.append(prec)\n        cv_recalls.append(rec)\n        try:\n            cv_aucs.append(roc_auc_score(y_val, y_proba))\n        except ValueError:\n            cv_aucs.append(0.5)\n\n    # Train final probe on all data\n    probe.fit(X_scaled, y)\n\n    return {\n        'probe': probe,\n        'scaler': scaler,\n        'cv_accuracy_mean': np.mean(cv_accuracies),\n        'cv_accuracy_std': np.std(cv_accuracies),\n        'cv_f1_mean': np.mean(cv_f1s),\n        'cv_f1_std': np.std(cv_f1s),\n        'cv_auc_mean': np.mean(cv_aucs),\n        'cv_auc_std': np.std(cv_aucs),\n        'cv_precision_mean': np.mean(cv_precisions),\n        'cv_recall_mean': np.mean(cv_recalls),\n        'cv_accuracies': cv_accuracies,\n        'cv_f1s': cv_f1s,\n        'cv_aucs': cv_aucs,\n    }\n\n\ndef main():\n    start_time = time.time()\n\n    # ==========================================\n    # Load data\n    # ==========================================\n    print(\"Loading data...\")\n    data = load_data()\n    texts = [item['text'] for item in data]\n    print(f\"Loaded {len(data)} examples\")\n\n    # ==========================================\n    # Step 1: Generate behavioral labels\n    # ==========================================\n    print(\"\\nLoading causal LM model for generation...\")\n    tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained(MODEL_NAME, trust_remote_code=True)\n    if tokenizer.pad_token is None:\n        tokenizer.pad_token = tokenizer.eos_token\n\n    gen_model = AutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained(\n        MODEL_NAME,\n        dtype=torch.float16,\n        trust_remote_code=True\n    ).cuda()\n\n    labels, responses = generate_behavioral_labels(data, tokenizer, gen_model)\n    save_behavioral_labels(data, labels)\n    labels = np.array(labels)\n\n    # Save responses for debugging\n    with open(WORK_DIR / 'model_responses.jsonl', 'w') as f:\n        for item, label, response in zip(data, labels, responses):\n            entry = {\n                \"text\": item['text'],\n                \"response\": response[:300],\n                \"label\": int(label),\n                \"correct_answers\": item['correct_answers']\n            }\n            f.write(json.dumps(entry) + '\\n')\n\n    print(f\"\\nLabel distribution: {np.sum(labels == 1)} 170→\n   171→    for i, item in enumerate(data):\n   172→        question = item['text']\n   173→        correct_answers = item['correct_answers']\n   174→\n   175→        # Format as a simple Q&A prompt\n   176→        prompt = f\"Q: {question}\\nA:\"\n   177→\n   178→        inputs = tokenizer(prompt, return_tensors=\"pt\", truncation=True, max_length=256)\n   179→        inputs = {k: v.cuda() for k, v in inputs.items()}\n   180→\n   181→        with torch.no_grad():\n   182→            outputs = model.generate(\n   183→                **inputs,\n   184→                max_new_tokens=80,\n   185→                do_sample=False,\n   186→                temperature=1.0,\n   187→                pad_token_id=tokenizer.eos_token_id,\n   188→            )\n   189→\n   190→        # Decode only the generated part\n   191→        input_len = inputs['input_ids'].shape[1]\n   192→        generated = tokenizer.decode(outputs[0][input_len:], skip_special_tokens=True).strip()\n   193→\n   194→        # Check correctness\n   195→        is_correct = check_answer_correctness(generated, correct_answers, question)\n   196→        label = 1 if is_correct else 0\n   197→        labels.append(label)\n   198→        responses.append(generated)\n   199→\n   200→        if is_correct:\n   201→            correct_count += 1\n   202→\n   203→        if i < 15 or (i < 100 and i % 25 == 0) or i % 100 == 0:\n   204→            print(f\"\\n[{i}/{len(data)}] Q: {question[:80]}...\")\n   205→            print(f\"  Generated: {generated[:120]}...\")\n   206→            print(f\"  Correct answers: {correct_answers[0][:80]}...\")\n   207→            print(f\"  Label: {label} ({'correct' if label else 'incorrect'})\")\n   208→\n   209→    print(f\"\\n{'=' * 40}\")\n   210→    print(f\"Total correct: {correct_count}/{len(data)} ({correct_count/len(data)*100:.1f}%)\")\n   211→    print(f\"Total incorrect: {len(data) - correct_count}/{len(data)} ({(len(data)-correct_count)/len(data)*100:.1f}%)\")\n   212→\n   213→    return labels, responses\n   214→\n   215→\n   216→def save_behavioral_labels(data, labels):\n   217→    \"\"\"Save behavioral labels to jsonl.\"\"\"\n   218→    with open(BEHAVIORAL_LABELS_FILE, 'w') as f:\n   219→        for item, label in zip(data, labels):\n   220→            entry = {\"text\": item['text'], \"label\": label}\n   221→            f.write(json.dumps(entry) + '\\n')\n   222→    print(f\"Saved behavioral labels to {BEHAVIORAL_LABELS_FILE}\")\n   223→\n   224→\n   225→def extract_activations_all_layers(base_model, tokenizer, texts, aggregation='mean', batch_size=16):\n   226→    \"\"\"\n   227→    Extract activations from all layers of the base model.\n   228→    Returns shape: (n_layers, n_samples, hidden_dim)\n   229→    \"\"\"\n   230→    base_model.eval()\n   231→    device = next(base_model.parameters()).device\n   232→\n   233→    all_layer_activations = None\n   234→    n_layers = None\n   235→\n   236→    for i in range(0, len(texts), batch_size):\n   237→        batch_texts = texts[i:i + batch_size]\n   238→\n   239→        with torch.no_grad():\n   240→            inputs = tokenizer(\n   241→                batch_texts,\n   242→                return_tensors=\"pt\",\n   243→                truncation=True,\n   244→                max_length=512,\n   245→                padding=True\n   246→            )\n   247→            inputs = {k: v.to(device) for k, v in inputs.items()}\n   248→            attention_mask = inputs.get('attention_mask', None)\n   249→\n   250→            outputs = base_model(**inputs, output_hidden_states=True)\n   251→            hidden_states = outputs.hidden_states  # Tuple of (batch, seq_len, hidden_dim)\n   252→\n   253→            if n_layers is None:\n   254→                n_layers = len(hidden_states)\n   255→                all_layer_activations = [[] for _ in range(n_layers)]\n   256→\n   257→            for layer_idx in range(n_layers):\n   258→                hs = hidden_states[layer_idx].cpu().float().numpy()  # (batch, seq_len, hidden_dim)\n   259→\n   260→                if aggregation == 'first':\n   261→                    act = hs[:, 0, :]\n   262→                elif aggregation == 'last':\n   263→                    # Use last non-padded token\n   264→                    if attention_mask is not None:\n   265→                        mask = attention_mask.cpu().numpy()\n   266→                        batch_act = []\n   267→                        for b in range(hs.shape[0]):\n   268→                            last_idx = int(mask[b].sum()) - 1\n   269→                            batch_act.append(hs[b, last_idx, :])\n   270→                        act = np.array(batch_act)\n   271→                    else:\n   272→                        act = hs[:, -1, :]\n   273→                elif aggregation == 'mean':\n   274→                    if attention_mask is not None:\n   275→                        mask = attention_mask.cpu().numpy()[:, :, None]  # (batch, seq_len, 1)\n   276→                        masked_hs = hs * mask\n   277→                        act = masked_hs.sum(axis=1) / np.maximum(mask.sum(axis=1), 1e-8)\n   278→                    else:\n   279→                        act = hs.mean(axis=1)\n   280→                elif aggregation == 'max':\n   281→                    if attention_mask is not None:\n   282→                        mask = attention_mask.cpu().numpy()[:, :, None]\n   283→                        masked_hs = hs * mask + (1 - mask) * (-1e9)\n   284→                        act = masked_hs.max(axis=1)\n   285→                    else:\n   286→                        act = hs.max(axis=1)\n   287→                else:\n   288→                    raise ValueError(f\"Unknown aggregation: {aggregation}\")\n   289→\n   290→                all_layer_activations[layer_idx].append(act)\n   291→\n   292→        if (i // batch_size) % 10 == 0:\n   293→            print(f\"  Processed {min(i + batch_size, len(texts))}/{len(texts)} texts\")\n   294→\n   295→    # Concatenate batches for each layer\n   296→    result = []\n   297→    for layer_idx in range(n_layers):\n   298→        result.append(np.concatenate(all_layer_activations[layer_idx], axis=0))\n   299→\n   300→    return np.array(result), n_layers\n   301→\n   302→\n   303→def train_and_evaluate_probe(X, y, cv_folds=5, max_iter=2000):\n   304→    \"\"\"Train a logistic regression probe with cross-validation.\"\"\"\n   305→    scaler = StandardScaler()\n   306→    X_scaled = scaler.fit_transform(X)\n   307→\n   308→    probe = LogisticRegression(max_iter=max_iter, random_state=42, C=1.0, solver='lbfgs')\n   309→\n   310→    skf = StratifiedKFold(n_splits=cv_folds, shuffle=True, random_state=42)\n   311→\n   312→    cv_accuracies = []\n   313→    cv_f1s = []\n   314→    cv_aucs = []\n   315→    cv_precisions = []\n   316→    cv_recalls = []\n   317→\n   318→    for train_idx, val_idx in skf.split(X_scaled, y):\n   319→        X_train, X_val = X_scaled[train_idx], X_scaled[val_idx]\n   320→        y_train, y_val = y[train_idx], y[val_idx]\n   321→\n   322→        probe_cv = LogisticRegression(max_iter=max_iter, random_state=42, C=1.0, solver='lbfgs')\n   323→        probe_cv.fit(X_train, y_train)\n   324→\n   325→        y_pred = probe_cv.predict(X_val)\n   326→        y_proba = probe_cv.predict_proba(X_val)[:, 1]\n   327→\n   328→        cv_accuracies.append(accuracy_score(y_val, y_pred))\n   329→        prec, rec, f1, _ = precision_recall_fscore_support(y_val, y_pred, average='binary', zero_division=0)\n   330→        cv_f1s.append(f1)\n   331→        cv_precisions.append(prec)\n   332→        cv_recalls.append(rec)\n   333→        try:\n   334→            cv_aucs.append(roc_auc_score(y_val, y_proba))\n   335→        except ValueError:\n   336→            cv_aucs.append(0.5)\n   337→\n   338→    # Train final probe on all data\n   339→    probe.fit(X_scaled, y)\n   340→\n   341→    return {\n   342→        'probe': probe,\n   343→        'scaler': scaler,\n   344→        'cv_accuracy_mean': np.mean(cv_accuracies),\n   345→        'cv_accuracy_std': np.std(cv_accuracies),\n   346→        'cv_f1_mean': np.mean(cv_f1s),\n   347→        'cv_f1_std': np.std(cv_f1s),\n   348→        'cv_auc_mean': np.mean(cv_aucs),\n   349→        'cv_auc_std': np.std(cv_aucs),\n   350→        'cv_precision_mean': np.mean(cv_precisions),\n   351→        'cv_recall_mean': np.mean(cv_recalls),\n   352→        'cv_accuracies': cv_accuracies,\n   353→        'cv_f1s': cv_f1s,\n   354→        'cv_aucs': cv_aucs,\n   355→    }\n   356→\n   357→\n   358→def main():\n   359→    start_time = time.time()\n   360→\n   361→    # ==========================================\n   362→    # Load data\n   363→    # ==========================================\n   364→    print(\"Loading data...\")\n   365→    data = load_data()\n   366→    texts = [item['text'] for item in data]\n   367→    print(f\"Loaded {len(data)} examples\")\n   368→\n   369→    # ==========================================\n   370→    # Step 1: Generate behavioral labels\n   371→    # ==========================================\n   372→    print(\"\\nLoading causal LM model for generation...\")\n   373→    tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained(MODEL_NAME, trust_remote_code=True)\n   374→    if tokenizer.pad_token is None:\n   375→        tokenizer.pad_token = tokenizer.eos_token\n   376→\n   377→    gen_model = AutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained(\n   378→        MODEL_NAME,\n   379→        dtype=torch.float16,\n   380→        trust_remote_code=True\n   381→    ).cuda()\n   382→\n   383→    labels, responses = generate_behavioral_labels(data, tokenizer, gen_model)\n   384→    save_behavioral_labels(data, labels)\n   385→    labels = np.array(labels)\n   386→\n   387→    # Save responses for debugging\n   388→    with open(WORK_DIR / 'model_responses.jsonl', 'w') as f:\n   389→        for item, label, response in zip(data, labels, responses):\n   390→            entry = {\n   391→                \"text\": item['text'],\n   392→                \"response\": response[:300],\n   393→                \"label\": int(label),\n   394→                \"correct_answers\": item['correct_answers']\n   395→            }\n   396→            f.write(json.dumps(entry) + '\\n')\n   397→\n   398→    print(f\"\\nLabel distribution: {np.sum(labels == 1)} correct, {np.sum(labels == 0)} incorrect\")\n   399→\n   400→    # Free generation model memory\n   401→    del gen_model\n   402→    torch.cuda.empty_cache()\n   403→\n   404→    elapsed = time.time() - start_time\n   405→    print(f\"\\nStep 1 complete. Time elapsed: {elapsed/60:.1f} minutes\")\n   406→\n   407→    # ==========================================\n   408→    # Step 2: Extract activations from base model\n   409→    # ==========================================\n   410→    print(\"\\n\" + \"=\" * 60)\n   411→    print(\"STEP 2: Extracting activations from all layers\")\n   412→    print(\"=\" * 60)\n   413→\n   414→    print(\"Loading base model for activation extraction...\")\n   415→    base_model = AutoModel.from_pretrained(\n   416→        MODEL_NAME,\n   417→        dtype=torch.float16,\n   418→        trust_remote_code=True\n   419→    ).cuda()\n   420→\n   421→    # Test aggregation strategies\n   422→    aggregation_methods = ['mean', 'last', 'first', 'max']\n   423→    all_results = {}  # {aggregation: {layer: probe_result}}\n   424→\n   425→    for agg_method in aggregation_methods:\n   426→        print(f\"\\n--- Extracting activations with aggregation='{agg_method}' ---\")\n   427→        activations, n_layers = extract_activations_all_layers(\n   428→            base_model, tokenizer, texts,\n   429→            aggregation=agg_method,\n   430→            batch_size=16\n   431→        )\n   432→        print(f\"Activations shape: {activations.shape} (n_layers={n_layers})\")\n   433→\n   434→        # ==========================================\n   435→        # Step 3: Train probes for all layers\n   436→        # ==========================================\n   437→        print(f\"\\n--- Training probes for all {n_layers} layers (agg='{agg_method}') ---\")\n   438→        layer_results = {}\n   439→\n   440→        for layer_idx in range(n_layers):\n   441→            X = activations[layer_idx]\n   442→            result = train_and_evaluate_probe(X, labels)\n   443→            result['layer'] = layer_idx\n   444→            result['aggregation'] = agg_method\n   445→            layer_results[layer_idx] = result\n   446→\n   447→            if layer_idx % 4 == 0 or layer_idx == n_layers - 1:\n   448→                print(f\"  Layer {layer_idx:2d}: CV Acc={result['cv_accuracy_mean']:.3f}±{result['cv_accuracy_std']:.3f}, \"\n   449→                      f\"F1={result['cv_f1_mean']:.3f}±{result['cv_f1_std']:.3f}, \"\n   450→                      f\"AUC={result['cv_auc_mean']:.3f}±{result['cv_auc_std']:.3f}\")\n   451→\n   452→        all_results[agg_method] = layer_results\n   453→\n   454→        elapsed = time.time() - start_time\n   455→        print(f\"\\nAggregation '{agg_method}' complete. Time elapsed: {elapsed/60:.1f} minutes\")\n   456→\n   457→    # Free base model\n   458→    del base_model\n   459→    del activations\n   460→    torch.cuda.empty_cache()\n   461→\n   462→    # ==========================================\n   463→    # Step 4: Find best probe\n   464→    # ==========================================\n   465→    print(\"\\n\" + \"=\" * 60)\n   466→    print(\"STEP 4: Finding best probe configuration\")\n   467→    print(\"=\" * 60)\n   468→\n   469→    best_config = None\n   470→    best_auc = -1\n   471→\n   472→    for agg_method, layer_results in all_results.items():\n   473→        for layer_idx, result in layer_results.items():\n   474→            if result['cv_auc_mean'] > best_auc:\n   475→                best_auc = result['cv_auc_mean']\n   476→                best_config = (agg_method, layer_idx, result)\n   477→\n   478→    best_agg, best_layer, best_result = best_config\n   479→    print(f\"\\nBest configuration:\")\n   480→    print(f\"  Aggregation: {best_agg}\")\n   481→    print(f\"  Layer: {best_layer}\")\n   482→    print(f\"  CV Accuracy: {best_result['cv_accuracy_mean']:.4f} ± {best_result['cv_accuracy_std']:.4f}\")\n   483→    print(f\"  CV F1: {best_result['cv_f1_mean']:.4f} ± {best_result['cv_f1_std']:.4f}\")\n   484→    print(f\"  CV AUC: {best_result['cv_auc_mean']:.4f} ± {best_result['cv_auc_std']:.4f}\")\n   485→\n   486→    # ==========================================\n   487→    # Save best probe\n   488→    # 'cv_auc_mean': best_result['cv_auc_mean'],\n   497→    }\n   498→\n   499→    probe_path = FINAL_PROBE_DIR / \"probe.pkl\"\n   500→    with open(probe_path, 'wb') as f:\n   501→        pickle.dump(probe_save_data, f)\n   502→    print(f\"Saved best probe to {probe_path}\")\n   503→\n   504→    # ==========================================\n   505→    # Step 5: Generate metrics and visualizations\n   506→    # ==========================================\n   507→    print(\"\\n\" + \"=\" * 60)\n   508→    print(\"STEP 5: Generating metrics and visualizations\")\n   509→    print(\"=\" * 60)\n   510→\n   511→    # Compile metrics\n   512→    metrics = {\n   513→        'best_layer': int(best_layer),\n   514→        'best_aggregation': best_agg,\n   515→        'best_cv_accuracy': float(best_result['cv_accuracy_mean']),\n   516→        'best_cv_accuracy_std': float(best_result['cv_accuracy_std']),\n   517→        'best_cv_f1': float(best_result['cv_f1_mean']),\n   518→        'best_cv_f1_std': float(best_result['cv_f1_std']),\n   519→        'best_cv_auc': float(best_result['cv_auc_mean']),\n   520→        'best_cv_auc_std': float(best_result['cv_auc_std']),\n   521→        'best_cv_precision': float(best_result['cv_precision_mean']),\n   522→        'best_cv_recall': 526→            'total': int(len(labels))\n   527→        },\n   528→        'all_layer_results': {}\n   529→    }\n   530→\n   531→    for agg_method, layer_results in all_results.items():\n   532→        metrics['all_layer_results'][agg_method] = {}\n   533→        for layer_idx, result in layer_results.items():\n   534→            metrics['all_layer_results'][agg_method][str(layer_idx)] = {\n   535→                'cv_accuracy_mean': float(result['cv_accuracy_mean']),\n   536→                'cv_accuracy_std': float(result['cv_accuracy_std']),\n   537→                'cv_f1_mean': float(result['cv_f1_mean']),\n   538→                'cv_f1_std': float(result['cv_f1_std']),\n   539→                'cv_auc_mean': float(result['cv_auc_mean']),\n   540→                'cv_auc_std': float(result['cv_auc_std']),\n   541→            }\n   542→\n   543→    with open(METRICS_FILE, 'w') as f:\n   544→        json.dump(metrics, f, indent=2)\n   545→    print(f\"Saved metrics to {METRICS_FILE}\")\n   546→\n   547→    # ==========================================\n   548→    # Visualization 1: Probe accuracy across layers\n   549→    # ==========================================\n   550→    n_layers_val = len(all_results[aggregation_methods[0]])\n   551→\n   552→    fig, axes = plt.subplots(1, 3, figsize=(18, 5))\n   553→\n   554→    for agg_method in aggregation_methods:\n   555→        layers = sorted(all_results[agg_method].keys())\n   556→        accs = [all_results[agg_method][l]['cv_accuracy_mean'] for l in layers]\n   557→        acc_stds = [all_results[agg_method][l]['cv_accuracy_std'] for l in layers]\n   558→        f1s = [all_results[agg_method][l]['cv_f1_mean'] for l in layers]\n   559→        f1_stds = axes[2].fill_between(layers,\n   576→                             [a - s for a, s in zip(aucs, auc_stds)],\n   577→                             [a + s for a, s in zip(aucs, auc_stds)],\n   578→                             alpha=0.15)\n   579→        axes[2].plot(layers, aucs, label=agg_method, marker='o', markersize=3)\n   580→\n   581→    axes[0].set_xlabel('Layer')\n   582→ axes[2].set_xlabel('Layer')\n   596→    axes[2].set_ylabel('CV ROC-AUC')\n   597→    axes[2].set_title('Probe ROC-AUC Across Layers')\n   598→    axes[2].legend()\n   599→    axes[2].axhline(y=0.5, AUC={best_auc:.3f})', fontsize=14)\n   603→    plt.tight_layout()\n   604→    plt.savefig(WORK_DIR / 'probe_performance_across_layers.png', dpi=150, bbox_inches='tight')\n   605→    plt.close()\n plt.savefig(WORK_DIR / 'aggregation_comparison.png', dpi=150, bbox_inches='tight')\n   645→    plt.close()\n   646→    print(\"Saved: aggregation_comparison.png\")\n   647→\n   648→    # ==========================================\n   649→    # Visualization 3: Heatmap of AUC across layers and aggregation methods\n   650→    # ==========================================\n   651→    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(14, 5))\n   652→\n   653→    auc_matrix = np.zeros((len(aggregation_methods), n_layers_val))\n   654→    for i, agg in enumerate(aggregation_methods):\n   655→        for l
