python3\n\"\"\"\nComplete pipeline for truth analysis probing on Qwen2.5-1.5B.\nStep 1: Generate behavioral labels by running model on TruthfulQA questions.\nStep 2: Extract activations from all layers.\nStep 3: Train linear probes across layers and token aggregation strategies.\nStep 4: Evaluate, visualize, and save best probe.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport json\nimport os\nimport pickle\nimport sys\nimport time\nimport re\nimport numpy as np\nimport torch\nfrom pathlib import Path\nfrom transformers import AutoModelForCausalLM, AutoTokenizer, AutoModel\nfrom sklearn.linear_model import LogisticRegression\nfrom sklearn.model_selection import cross_val_score, StratifiedKFold\nfrom sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler\nfrom sklearn.metrics import (\n    accuracy_score, precision_recall_fscore_support,\n    roc_auc_score, classification_report, roc_curve\n)\nimport matplotlib\nmatplotlib.use('Agg')\nimport matplotlib.pyplot as plt\n\nWORK_DIR = Path(\"/iopsstor/scratch/cscs/oyasunaga/autointerp_runs/jobs/truth_analysis_Qwen_Qwen2.5-1.5B_2513489\")\nMODEL_NAME = \"Qwen/Qwen2.5-1.5B\"\nDATA_FILE = WORK_DIR / \"labeled_data.jsonl\"\nBEHAVIORAL_LABELS_FILE = WORK_DIR / \"behavioral_labels.jsonl\"\nFINAL_PROBE_DIR = WORK_DIR / \"final_probe\"\nMETRICS_FILE = WORK_DIR / \"metrics.json\"\n\nos.makedirs(FINAL_PROBE_DIR, exist_ok=True)\n\n\ndef load_data():\n    \"\"\"Load labeled data from jsonl.\"\"\"\n    data = []\n    with open(DATA_FILE, 'r') as f:\n        for line in f:\n            data.append(json.loads(line))\n    return data\n\n\ndef get_yes_no_stance(text):\n    \"\"\"\n    Determine if text has a clear yes/no stance.\n    Returns 'yes', 'no', or None.\n    \"\"\"\n    text_lower = text.lower().strip()\n    # Check first word/phrase\n    first_part = text_lower[:50]\n\n    # Strong yes indicators\n    if re.match(r'^(yes|yeah|yep|correct|absolutely|indeed|of course|sure|definitely|certainly|right)\\b', first_part):\n        return 'yes'\n\n    # Strong no indicators\n    if re.match(r'^(no|nope|not|nah|incorrect|wrong|neither|none|never)\\b', first_part):\n        return 'no'\n\n    # Check for \"X is not\" or \"X does not\" patterns\n    if re.search(r'\\b(is not|isn\\'t|are not|aren\\'t|does not|doesn\\'t|do not|don\\'t|cannot|can\\'t|has not|hasn\\'t|have not|haven\\'t|was not|wasn\\'t|were not|weren\\'t)\\b', first_part):\n        return 'no'\n\n    return None\n\n\ndef check_answer_correctness(model_response, correct_answers, question):\n    \"\"\"\n    Check if the model's response matches any correct answer.\n    Uses multiple strategies:\n    1. Yes/No direction matching for yes/no questions\n    2. Key entity/fact matching\n    3. Semantic content matching\n    \"\"\"\n    response_lower = model_response.lower().strip()\n    # Truncate response to first meaningful sentence\n    # Many responses go on tangents after the first sentence\n    first_sentence = response_lower.split('\\n')[0].strip()\n    if len(first_sentence) < 5:\n        first_sentence = response_lower[:200]\n\n    # Strategy 1: Yes/No direction matching\n    response_stance = get_yes_no_stance(first_sentence)\n    if response_stance is not None:\n        for correct in correct_answers:\n            correct_stance = get_yes_no_stance(correct.lower())\n            if correct_stance is not None:\n                # Both have a stance - check if they match\n                if response_stance == correct_stance:\n                    return True\n                else:\n                    return False\n\n    # Strategy 2: Check for key factual content\n    # Extract key content words from correct answers (removing common words)\n    stop_words = {'the', 'a', 'an', 'is', 'are', 'was', 'were', 'be', 'been', 'being',\n                  'have', 'has', 'had', 'do', 'does', 'did', 'will', 'would', 'could',\n                  'should', 'may', 'might', 'can', 'shall', 'must', 'need', 'dare',\n                  'to', 'of', 'in', 'for', 'on', 'with', 'at', 'by', 'from', 'as',\n                  'into', 'through', 'during', 'before', 'after', 'above', 'below',\n                  'between', 'out', 'off', 'over', 'under', 'again', 'further',\n                  'then', 'once', 'and', 'but', 'or', 'nor', 'not', 'so', 'yet',\n                  'both', 'each', 'few', 'more', 'most', 'other', 'some', 'such',\n                  'only', 'own', 'same', 'than', 'too', 'very', 'just', 'because',\n                  'that', 'this', 'these', 'those', 'it', 'its', 'they', 'them',\n                  'their', 'we', 'our', 'you', 'your', 'he', 'she', 'him', 'her',\n                  'his', 'who', 'which', 'what', 'when', 'where', 'how', 'why',\n                  'all', 'any', 'no', 'yes', 'if', 'about', 'up', 'there', 'here',\n                  'also', 'said', 'says', 'say'}\n\n    best_match_score = 0\n\n    for correct in correct_answers:\n        correct_lower = correct.lower().strip()\n\n        # Direct substring matching (relaxed)\n        # Remove common phrases from correct answer\n        correct_core = re.sub(r'^(yes|no|no,|yes,)\\s*', '', correct_lower).strip()\n\n        if correct_core in first_sentence or first_sentence in correct_core:\n            return True\n\n        # Key word matching\n        correct_words = set(re.findall(r'\\b[a-z]+\\b', correct_lower)) - stop_words\n        response_words = set(re.findall(r'\\b[a-z]+\\b', first_sentence)) - stop_words\n\n        if len(correct_words) > 0:\n            # Check overlap of correct words found in response\n            overlap = correct_words & response_words\n            score = len(overlap) / len(correct_words)\n            best_match_score = max(best_match_score, score)\n\n    # Strategy 3: Check for \"I have no comment\" or uncertainty markers (often correct for TruthfulQA)\n    uncertainty_markers = ['i have no comment', 'i don\\'t know', 'i\\'m not sure',\n                           'it\\'s unclear', 'there is no evidence', 'uncertain',\n                           'it depends', 'cannot be determined']\n    for marker in uncertainty_markers:\n        if marker in first_sentence:\n            for correct in correct_answers:\n                if any(um in correct.lower() for um in ['no comment', 'uncertain', 'unclear', 'ambiguous']):\n                    return True\n\n    # Threshold for key word matching\n    if best_match_score >= 0.5:\n        return True\n\n    return False\n\n\ndef generate_behavioral_labels(data, tokenizer, model):\n    \"\"\"\n    Generate behavioral labels by running the model on each question.\n    label=1 if model answers correctly, label=0 if incorrect.\n    \"\"\"\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n    print(\"STEP 1: Generating behavioral labels\")\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n\n    model.eval()\n    labels = []\n    correct_count = 0\n    responses = []\n\n    for i, item in enumerate(data):\n        question = item['text']\n        correct_answers = item['correct_answers']\n\n        # Format as a simple Q&A prompt\n        prompt = f\"Q: {question}\\nA:\"\n\n        inputs = tokenizer(prompt, return_tensors=\"pt\", truncation=True, max_length=256)\n        inputs = {k: v.cuda() for k, v in inputs.items()}\n\n        with torch.no_grad():\n            outputs = model.generate(\n                **inputs,\n                max_new_tokens=80,\n                do_sample=False,\n                temperature=1.0,\n                pad_token_id=tokenizer.eos_token_id,\n            )\n\n        # Decode only the generated part\n        input_len = inputs['input_ids'].shape[1]\n        generated = tokenizer.decode(outputs[0][input_len:], skip_special_tokens=True).strip()\n\n        # Check correctness\n        is_correct = check_answer_correctness(generated, correct_answers, question)\n        label = 1 if is_correct else 0\n        labels.append(label)\n        responses.append(generated)\n\n        if is_correct:\n            correct_count += 1\n\n        if i < 15 or (i < 100 and i % 25 == 0) or i % 100 == 0:\n            print(f\"\\n[{i}/{len(data)}] Q: {question[:80]}...\")\n            print(f\"  Generated: {generated[:120]}...\")\n            print(f\"  Correct answers: {correct_answers[0][:80]}...\")\n            print(f\"  Label: {label} ({'correct' if label else 'incorrect'})\")\n\n    print(f\"\\n{'=' * 40}\")\n    print(f\"Total correct: {correct_count}/{len(data)} ({correct_count/len(data)*100:.1f}%)\")\n    print(f\"Total incorrect: {len(data) - correct_count}/{len(data)} ({(len(data)-correct_count)/len(data)*100:.1f}%)\")\n\n    return labels, responses\n\n\ndef save_behavioral_labels(data, labels):\n    \"\"\"Save behavioral labels to jsonl.\"\"\"\n    with open(BEHAVIORAL_LABELS_FILE, 'w') as f:\n        for item, label in zip(data, labels):\n            entry = {\"text\": item['text'], \"label\": label}\n            f.write(json.dumps(entry) + '\\n')\n    print(f\"Saved behavioral labels to {BEHAVIORAL_LABELS_FILE}\")\n\n\ndef extract_activations_all_layers(base_model, tokenizer, texts, aggregation='mean', batch_size=16):\n    \"\"\"\n    Extract activations from all layers of the base model.\n    Returns shape: (n_layers, n_samples, hidden_dim)\n    \"\"\"\n    base_model.eval()\n    device = next(base_model.parameters()).device\n\n    all_layer_activations = None\n    n_layers = None\n\n    for i in range(0, len(texts), batch_size):\n        batch_texts = texts[i:i + batch_size]\n\n        with torch.no_grad():\n            inputs = tokenizer(\n                batch_texts,\n                return_tensors=\"pt\",\n                truncation=True,\n                max_length=512,\n                padding=True\n            )\n            inputs = {k: v.to(device) for k, v in inputs.items()}\n            attention_mask = inputs.get('attention_mask', None)\n\n            outputs = base_model(**inputs, output_hidden_states=True)\n            hidden_states = outputs.hidden_states  # Tuple of (batch, seq_len, hidden_dim)\n\n            if n_layers is None:\n                n_layers = len(hidden_states)\n                all_layer_activations = [[] for _ in range(n_layers)]\n\n            for layer_idx in range(n_layers):\n                hs = hidden_states[layer_idx].cpu().float().numpy()  # (batch, seq_len, hidden_dim)\n\n                if aggregation == 'first':\n                    act = hs[:, 0, :]\n                elif aggregation == 'last':\n                    # Use last non-padded token\n                    if attention_mask is not None:\n                        mask = attention_mask.cpu().numpy()\n                        batch_act = []\n                        for b in range(hs.shape[0]):\n                            last_idx = int(mask[b].sum()) - 1\n                            batch_act.append(hs[b, last_idx, :])\n                        act = np.array(batch_act)\n                    else:\n                        act = hs[:, -1, :]\n                elif aggregation == 'mean':\n                    if attention_mask is not None:\n                        mask = attention_mask.cpu().numpy()[:, :, None]  # (batch, seq_len, 1)\n                        masked_hs = hs * mask\n                        act = masked_hs.sum(axis=1) / np.maximum(mask.sum(axis=1), 1e-8)\n                    else:\n                        act = hs.mean(axis=1)\n                elif aggregation == 'max':\n                    if attention_mask is not None:\n                        mask = attention_mask.cpu().numpy()[:, :, None]\n                        masked_hs = hs * mask + (1 - mask) * (-1e9)\n                        act = masked_hs.max(axis=1)\n                    else:\n                        act = hs.max(axis=1)\n                else:\n                    raise ValueError(f\"Unknown aggregation: {aggregation}\")\n\n                all_layer_activations[layer_idx].append(act)\n\n        if (i // batch_size) % 10 == 0:\n            print(f\"  Processed {min(i + batch_size, len(texts))}/{len(texts)} texts\")\n\n    # Concatenate batches for each layer\n    result = []\n    for layer_idx in range(n_layers):\n        result.append(np.concatenate(all_layer_activations[layer_idx], axis=0))\n\n    return np.array(result), n_layers\n\n\ndef train_and_evaluate_probe(X, y, cv_folds=5, max_iter=2000):\n    \"\"\"Train a logistic regression probe with cross-validation.\"\"\"\n    scaler = StandardScaler()\n    X_scaled = scaler.fit_transform(X)\n\n    probe = LogisticRegression(max_iter=max_iter, random_state=42, C=1.0, solver='lbfgs')\n\n    skf = StratifiedKFold(n_splits=cv_folds, shuffle=True, random_state=42)\n\n    cv_accuracies = []\n    cv_f1s = []\n    cv_aucs = []\n    cv_precisions = []\n    cv_recalls = []\n\n    for train_idx, val_idx in skf.split(X_scaled, y):\n        X_train, X_val = X_scaled[train_idx], X_scaled[val_idx]\n        y_train, y_val = y[train_idx], y[val_idx]\n\n        probe_cv = LogisticRegression(max_iter=max_iter, random_state=42, C=1.0, solver='lbfgs')\n        probe_cv.fit(X_train, y_train)\n\n        y_pred = probe_cv.predict(X_val)\n        y_proba = probe_cv.predict_proba(X_val)[:, 1]\n\n        cv_accuracies.append(accuracy_score(y_val, y_pred))\n        prec, rec, f1, _ = precision_recall_fscore_support(y_val, y_pred, average='binary', zero_division=0)\n        cv_f1s.append(f1)\n        cv_precisions.append(prec)\n        cv_recalls.append(rec)\n        try:\n            cv_aucs.append(roc_auc_score(y_val, y_proba))\n        except ValueError:\n            cv_aucs.append(0.5)\n\n    # Train final probe on all data\n    probe.fit(X_scaled, y)\n\n    return {\n        'probe': probe,\n        'scaler': scaler,\n        'cv_accuracy_mean': np.mean(cv_accuracies),\n        'cv_accuracy_std': np.std(cv_accuracies),\n        'cv_f1_mean': np.mean(cv_f1s),\n        'cv_f1_std': np.std(cv_f1s),\n        'cv_auc_mean': np.mean(cv_aucs),\n        'cv_auc_std': np.std(cv_aucs),\n        'cv_precision_mean': np.mean(cv_precisions),\n        'cv_recall_mean': np.mean(cv_recalls),\n        'cv_accuracies': cv_accuracies,\n        'cv_f1s': cv_f1s,\n        'cv_aucs': cv_aucs,\n    }\n\n\ndef main():\n    start_time = time.time()\n\n    # ==========================================\n    # Load data\n    # ==========================================\n    print(\"Loading data...\")\n    data = load_data()\n    texts = [item['text'] for item in data]\n    print(f\"Loaded {len(data)} examples\")\n\n    # ==========================================\n    # Step 1: Generate behavioral labels\n    # ==========================================\n    print(\"\\nLoading causal LM model for generation...\")\n    tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained(MODEL_NAME, trust_remote_code=True)\n    if tokenizer.pad_token is None:\n        tokenizer.pad_token = tokenizer.eos_token\n\n    gen_model = AutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained(\n        MODEL_NAME,\n        dtype=torch.float16,\n        trust_remote_code=True\n    ).cuda()\n\n    labels, responses = generate_behavioral_labels(data, tokenizer, gen_model)\n    save_behavioral_labels(data, labels)\n    labels = np.array(labels)\n\n    # Save responses for debugging\n    with open(WORK_DIR / 'model_responses.jsonl', 'w') as f:\n        for item, label, response in zip(data, labels, responses):\n            entry = {\n                \"text\": item['text'],\n                \"response\": response[:300],\n                \"label\": int(label),\n                \"correct_answers\": item['correct_answers']\n            }\n            f.write(json.dumps(entry) + '\\n')\n\n    print(f\"\\nLabel distribution: {np.sum(labels == 1)} correct, {np.sum(labels == 0)} incorrect\")\n\n    # Free generation model memory\n    del gen_model\n    torch.cuda.empty_cache()\n\n    elapsed = time.time() - start_time\n    print(f\"\\nStep 1 complete. Time elapsed: {elapsed/60:.1f} minutes\")\n\n    # ==========================================\n    # Step 2: Extract activations from base model\n    # ==========================================\n    print(\"\\n\" + \"=\" * 60)\n    print(\"STEP 2: Extracting activations from all layers\")\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n\n    print(\"Loading base model for activation extraction...\")\n    base_model = AutoModel.from_pretrained(\n        MODEL_NAME,\n        dtype=torch.float16,\n        trust_remote_code=True\n    ).cuda()\n\n    # Test aggregation strategies\n    aggregation_methods = ['mean', 'last', 'first', 'max']\n    all_results = {}  # {aggregation: {layer: probe_result}}\n\n    for agg_method in aggregation_methods:\n        print(f\"\\n--- Extracting activations with aggregation='{agg_method}' ---\")\n        activations, n_layers = extract_activations_all_layers(\n            base_model, tokenizer, texts,\n            aggregation=agg_method,\n            batch_size=16\n        )\n        print(f\"Activations shape: {activations.shape} (n_layers={n_layers})\")\n\n        # ==========================================\n        # Step 3: Train probes for all layers\n        # ==========================================\n        print(f\"\\n--- Training probes for all {n_layers} layers (agg='{agg_method}') ---\")\n        layer_results = {}\n\n        for layer_idx in range(n_layers):\n            X = activations[layer_idx]\n            result = train_and_evaluate_probe(X, labels)\n            result['layer'] = layer_idx\n            result['aggregation'] = agg_method\n            layer_results[layer_idx] = result\n\n            if layer_idx % 4 == 0 or layer_idx == n_layers - 1:\n                print(f\"  Layer {layer_idx:2d}: CV Acc={result['cv_accuracy_mean']:.3f}±{result['cv_accuracy_std']:.3f}, \"\n                      f\"F1={result['cv_f1_mean']:.3f}±{result['cv_f1_std']:.3f}, \"\n                      f\"AUC={result['cv_auc_mean']:.3f}±{result['cv_auc_std']:.3f}\")\n\n        all_results[agg_method] = layer_results\n\n        elapsed = time.time() - start_time\n        print(f\"\\nAggregation '{agg_method}' complete. Time elapsed: {elapsed/60:.1f} minutes\")\n\n    # Free base model\n    del base_model\n    del activations\n    torch.cuda.empty_cache()\n\n    # ==========================================\n    # Step 4: Find best probe\n    # ==========================================\n    print(\"\\n\" + \"=\" * 60)\n    print(\"STEP 4: Finding best probe configuration\")\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n\n    best_config = None\n    best_auc = -1\n\n    for agg_method, layer_results in all_results.items():\n        for layer_idx, result in layer_results.items():\n            if result['cv_auc_mean'] > best_auc:\n                best_auc = result['cv_auc_mean']\n                best_config = (agg_method, layer_idx, result)\n\n    best_agg, best_layer, best_result = best_config\n    print(f\"\\nBest configuration:\")\n    print(f\"  Aggregation: {best_agg}\")\n    print(f\"  Layer: {best_layer}\")\n    print(f\"  CV Accuracy: {best_result['cv_accuracy_mean']:.4f} ± {best_result['cv_accuracy_std']:.4f}\")\n    print(f\"  CV F1: {best_result['cv_f1_mean']:.4f} ± {best_result['cv_f1_std']:.4f}\")\n    print(f\"  CV AUC: {best_result['cv_auc_mean']:.4f} ± {best_result['cv_auc_std']:.4f}\")\n\n    # ==========================================\n    # Save best probe\n    # ==========================================\n    probe_save_data = {\n        'model': best_result['probe'],\n        'scaler': best_result['scaler'],\n        'layer': best_layer,\n        'aggregation': best_agg,\n        'cv_accuracy_mean': best_result['cv_accuracy_mean'],\n \"Qwen/Qwen2.5-1.5B\"\nDATA_FILE = WORK_DIR / \"labeled_data.jsonl\"\nBEHAVIORAL_LABELS_FILE = WORK_DIR / \"behavioral_labels.jsonl\"\nFINAL_PROBE_DIR = WORK_DIR / \"final_probe\"\nMETRICS_FILE = WORK_DIR / \"metrics.json\"\n\nos.makedirs(FINAL_PROBE_DIR, exist_ok=True)\n\n\ndef load_data():\n    \"\"\"Load labeled data from jsonl.\"\"\"\n    data = []\n    with open(DATA_FILE, 'r') as f:\n        for line in f:\n            data.append(json.loads(line))\n    return data\n\n\ndef normalize_text(text):\n    \"\"\"Normalize text for comparison.\"\"\"\n    text = text.lower().strip()\n    # Remove punctuation at end\n    text = re.sub(r'[.,;:!?\\s]+$', '', text)\n    # Remove articles at start\n    text = re.sub(r'^(the|a|an)\\s+', '', text)\n    return text\n\n\ndef check_answer_correctness(model_response, correct_answers):\n    \"\"\"\n    Check if the model's response matches any correct answer.\n    Uses flexible matching: checks if any correct answer is contained\n    in the model response or vice versa.\n    \"\"\"\n    response_lower = model_response.lower().strip()\n    response_normalized = normalize_text(response_lower)\n\n    for correct in correct_answers:\n        correct_lower = correct.lower().strip()\n        correct_normalized = normalize_text(correct_lower)\n\n        # Direct containment check\n        if correct_normalized in response_normalized:\n            return True\n        if response_normalized in correct_normalized:\n            return True\n\n        # Check key phrases (extract important words)\n        # Split correct answer into significant words (>3 chars)\n        key_words = [w for w in correct_normalized.split() if len(w) > 3]\n        if len(key_words) >= 2:\n            matches = sum(1 for w in key_words if w in response_normalized)\n            if matches >= len(key_words) * 0.6:\n                return True\n\n    return False\n\n\ndef generate_behavioral_labels(data, tokenizer, model):\n    \"\"\"\n    Generate behavioral labels by running the model on each question.\n    label=1 if model answers correctly, label=0 if incorrect.\n    \"\"\"\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n    print(\"STEP 1: Generating behavioral labels\")\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n\n    model.eval()\n    labels = []\n    correct_count = 0\n\n    for i, item in enumerate(data):\n        question = item['text']\n        correct_answers = item['correct_answers']\n\n        # Format as a simple Q&A prompt\n        prompt = f\"Q: {question}\\nA:\"\n\n        inputs = tokenizer(prompt, return_tensors=\"pt\", truncation=True, max_length=256)\n        inputs = {k: v.cuda() for k, v in inputs.items()}\n\n        with torch.no_grad():\n            outputs = model.generate(\n                **inputs,\n                max_new_tokens=100,\n                do_sample=False,\n                temperature=1.0,\n                pad_token_id=tokenizer.eos_token_id,\n            )\n\n        # Decode only the generated part\n        input_len = inputs['input_ids'].shape[1]\n        generated = tokenizer.decode(outputs[0][input_len:], skip_special_tokens=True).strip()\n\n        # Check correctness\n        is_correct = check_answer_correctness(generated, correct_answers)\n        label = 1 if is_correct else 0\n        labels.append(label)\n\n        if is_correct:\n            correct_count += 1\n\n        if i < 10 or (i < 100 and i % 20 == 0) or i % 100 == 0:\n            print(f\"\\n[{i}/{len(data)}] Q: {question[:80]}...\")\n            print(f\"  Generated: {generated[:120]}...\")\n            print(f\"  Correct answers: {correct_answers[0][:80]}...\")\n            print(f\"  Label: {label} ({'correct' if label else 'incorrect'})\")\n\n    print(f\"\\n{'=' * 40}\")\n    print(f\"Total correct: {correct_count}/{len(data)} ({correct_count/len(data)*100:.1f}%)\")\n    print(f\"Total incorrect: {len(data) - correct_count}/{len(data)} ({(len(data)-correct_count)/len(data)*100:.1f}%)\")\n\n    return labels\n\n\ndef save_behavioral_labels(data, labels):\n    \"\"\"Save behavioral labels to jsonl.\"\"\"\n    with open(BEHAVIORAL_LABELS_FILE, 'w') as f:\n        for item, label in zip(data, labels):\n            entry = {\"text\": item['text'], \"label\": label}\n            f.write(json.dumps(entry) + '\\n')\n    print(f\"Saved behavioral labels to {BEHAVIORAL_LABELS_FILE}\")\n\n\ndef extract_activations_all_layers(base_model, tokenizer, texts, aggregation='mean', batch_size=16):\n    \"\"\"\n    Extract activations from all layers of the base model.\n    Returns shape: (n_layers, n_samples, hidden_dim)\n    \"\"\"\n    base_model.eval()\n    device = next(base_model.parameters()).device\n\n    all_layer_activations = None\n    n_layers = None\n\n    for i in range(0, len(texts), batch_size):\n        batch_texts = texts[i:i + batch_size]\n\n        with torch.no_grad():\n            inputs = tokenizer(\n                batch_texts,\n                return_tensors=\"pt\",\n                truncation=True,\n                max_length=512,\n                padding=True\n            )\n            inputs = {k: v.to(device) for k, v in inputs.items()}\n            attention_mask = inputs.get('attention_mask', None)\n\n            outputs = base_model(**inputs, output_hidden_states=True)\n            hidden_states = outputs.hidden_states  # Tuple of (batch, seq_len, hidden_dim)\n\n            if n_layers is None:\n                n_layers = len(hidden_states)\n                all_layer_activations = [[] for _ in range(n_layers)]\n\n            for layer_idx in range(n_layers):\n                hs = hidden_states[layer_idx].cpu().float().numpy()  # (batch, seq_len, hidden_dim)\n\n                if aggregation == 'first':\n                    act = hs[:, 0, :]\n                elif aggregation == 'last':\n                    # Use last non-padded token\n                    if attention_mask is not None:\n                        mask = attention_mask.cpu().numpy()\n                        batch_act = []\n                        for b in range(hs.shape[0]):\n                            last_idx = int(mask[b].sum()) - 1\n                            batch_act.append(hs[b, last_idx, :])\n                        act = np.array(batch_act)\n                    else:\n                        act = hs[:, -1, :]\n                elif aggregation == 'mean':\n                    if attention_mask is not None:\n                        mask = attention_mask.cpu().numpy()[:, :, None]  # (batch, seq_len, 1)\n                        masked_hs = hs * mask\n                        act = masked_hs.sum(axis=1) / mask.sum(axis=1)\n                    else:\n                        act = hs.mean(axis=1)\n                elif aggregation == 'max':\n                    if attention_mask is not None:\n                        mask = attention_mask.cpu().numpy()[:, :, None]\n                        masked_hs = hs * mask + (1 - mask) * (-1e9)\n                        act = masked_hs.max(axis=1)\n                    else:\n                        act = hs.max(axis=1)\n                else:\n                    raise ValueError(f\"Unknown aggregation: {aggregation}\")\n\n                all_layer_activations[layer_idx].append(act)\n\n        if (i // batch_size) % 10 == 0:\n            print(f\"  Processed {min(i + batch_size, len(texts))}/{len(texts)} texts\")\n\n    # Concatenate batches for each layer\n    result = []\n    for layer_idx in range(n_layers):\n        result.append(np.concatenate(all_layer_activations[layer_idx], axis=0))\n\n    return np.array(result), n_layers\n\n\ndef train_and_evaluate_probe(X, y, cv_folds=5, max_iter=2000):\n    \"\"\"Train a logistic regression probe with cross-validation.\"\"\"\n    scaler = StandardScaler()\n    X_scaled = scaler.fit_transform(X)\n\n    probe = LogisticRegression(max_iter=max_iter, random_state=42, C=1.0, solver='lbfgs')\n\n    skf = StratifiedKFold(n_splits=cv_folds, shuffle=True, random_state=42)\n\n    cv_accuracies = []\n    cv_f1s = []\n    cv_aucs = []\n\n    for train_idx, val_idx in skf.split(X_scaled, y):\n        X_train, X_val = X_scaled[train_idx], X_scaled[val_idx]\n        y_train, y_val = y[train_idx], y[val_idx]\n\n        probe_cv = LogisticRegression(max_iter=max_iter, random_state=42, C=1.0, solver='lbfgs')\n        probe_cv.fit(X_train, y_train)\n\n        y_pred = probe_cv.predict(X_val)\n        y_proba = probe_cv.predict_proba(X_val)[:, 1]\n\n        cv_accuracies.append(accuracy_score(y_val, y_pred))\n        _, _, f1, _ = precision_recall_fscore_support(y_val, y_pred, average='binary', zero_division=0)\n        cv_f1s.append(f1)\n        try:\n            cv_aucs.append(roc_auc_score(y_val, y_proba))\n        except ValueError:\n            cv_aucs.append(0.5)\n\n    # Train final probe on all data\n    probe.fit(X_scaled, y)\n\n    return {\n        'probe': probe,\n        'scaler': scaler,\n        'cv_accuracy_mean': np.mean(cv_accuracies),\n        'cv_accuracy_std': np.std(cv_accuracies),\n        'cv_f1_mean': np.mean(cv_f1s),\n        'cv_f1_std': np.std(cv_f1s),\n        'cv_auc_mean': np.mean(cv_aucs),\n        'cv_auc_std': np.std(cv_aucs),\n        'cv_accuracies': cv_accuracies,\n        'cv_f1s': cv_f1s,\n        'cv_aucs': cv_aucs,\n    }\n\n\ndef main():\n    start_time = time.time()\n\n    # ==========================================\n    # Load data\n    # ==========================================\n    print(\"Loading data...\")\n    data = load_data()\n    texts = [item['text'] for item in data]\n    print(f\"Loaded {len(data)} examples\")\n\n    # ==========================================\n    # Step 1: Generate behavioral labels\n    # ==========================================\n    print(\"\\nLoading causal LM model for generation...\")\n    tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained(MODEL_NAME, trust_remote_code=True)\n    if tokenizer.pad_token is None:\n        tokenizer.pad_token = tokenizer.eos_token\n\n    gen_model = AutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained(\n        MODEL_NAME,\n        torch_dtype=torch.float16,\n        trust_remote_code=True\n    ).cuda()\n\n    labels = generate_behavioral_labels(data, tokenizer, gen_model)\n    save_behavioral_labels(data, labels)\n    labels = np.array(labels)\n\n    print(f\"\\nLabel distribution: {np.sum(labels == 1)} correct, {np.sum(labels == 0)} incorrect\")\n\n    # Free generation model memory\n    del gen_model\n    torch.cuda.empty_cache()\n\n    elapsed = time.time() - start_time\n    print(f\"\\nStep 1 complete. Time elapsed: {elapsed/60:.1f} minutes\")\n\n    # ==========================================\n    # Step 2: Extract activations from base model\n    # ==========================================\n    print(\"\\n\" + \"=\" * 60)\n    print(\"STEP 2: Extracting activations from all layers\")\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n\n    print(\"Loading base model for activation extraction...\")\n    base_model = AutoModel.from_pretrained(\n        MODEL_NAME,\n        torch_dtype=torch.float16,\n        trust_remote_code=True\n    ).cuda()\n\n    # Test aggregation strategies\n    aggregation_methods = ['mean', 'last', 'first', 'max']\n    all_results = {}  # {aggregation: {layer: probe_result}}\n\n    for agg_method in aggregation_methods:\n        print(f\"\\n--- Extracting activations with aggregation='{agg_method}' ---\")\n        activations, n_layers = extract_activations_all_layers(\n            base_model, tokenizer, texts,\n            aggregation=agg_method,\n            batch_size=16\n        )\n        print(f\"Activations shape: {activations.shape} (n_layers={n_layers})\")\n\n        # ==========================================\n        # Step 3: Train probes for all layers\n        # ==========================================\n        print(f\"\\n--- Training probes for all {n_layers} layers (agg='{agg_method}') ---\")\n        layer_results = {}\n\n        for layer_idx in range(n_layers):\n            X = activations[layer_idx]\n            result = train_and_evaluate_probe(X, labels)\n            result['layer'] = layer_idx\n            result['aggregation'] = agg_method\n            layer_results[layer_idx] = result\n\n            if layer_idx % 4 == 0 or layer_idx == n_layers - 1:\n                print(f\"  Layer {layer_idx:2d}: CV Acc={result['cv_accuracy_mean']:.3f}±{result['cv_accuracy_std']:.3f}, \"\n                      f\"F1={result['cv_f1_mean']:.3f}±{result['cv_f1_std']:.3f}, \"\n                      f\"AUC={result['cv_auc_mean']:.3f}±{result['cv_auc_std']:.3f}\")\n\n        all_results[agg_method] = layer_results\n\n        elapsed = time.time() - start_time\n        print(f\"\\nAggregation '{agg_method}' complete. Time elapsed: {elapsed/60:.1f} minutes\")\n\n    # Free base model\n    del base_model\n    del activations\n    torch.cuda.empty_cache()\n\n    # ==========================================\n    # Step 4: Find best probe\n    # ==========================================\n    print(\"\\n\" + \"=\" * 60)\n    print(\"STEP 4: Finding best probe configuration\")\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n\n    best_config = None\n    best_auc = -1\n\n    for agg_method, layer_results in all_results.items():\n        for layer_idx, result in layer_results.items():\n            if result['cv_auc_mean'] > best_auc:\n                best_auc = result['cv_auc_mean']\n                best_config = (agg_method, layer_idx, result)\n\n    best_agg, best_layer, best_result = best_config\n    print(f\"\\nBest configuration:\")\n    print(f\"  Aggregation: {best_agg}\")\n    print(f\"  Layer: {best_layer}\")\n    print(f\"  CV Accuracy: {best_result['cv_accuracy_mean']:.4f} ± {best_result['cv_accuracy_std']:.4f}\")\n    print(f\"  CV F1: {best_result['cv_f1_mean']:.4f} ± {best_result['cv_f1_std']:.4f}\")\n    print(f\"  CV AUC: {best_result['cv_auc_mean']:.4f} ± {best_result['cv_auc_std']:.4f}\")\n\n    # ==========================================\n    # Save best probe\n    # ==========================================\n    probe_save_data = {\n        'model': best_result['probe'],\n        'scaler': best_result['scaler'],\n        'layer': best_layer,\n        'aggregation': best_agg,\n        'cv_accuracy_mean': best_result['cv_accuracy_mean'],\n        'cv_f1_mean': best_result['cv_f1_mean'],\n        'cv_auc_mean': best_result['cv_auc_mean'],\n    }\n\n    probe_path = FINAL_PROBE_DIR / \"probe.pkl\"\n    with open(probe_path, 'wb') as f:\n        pickle.dump(probe_save_data, f)\n    print(f\"Saved best probe to {probe_path}\")\n\n    # ==========================================\n    # Step 5: Generate metrics and visualizations\n    # ==========================================\n    print(\"\\n\" + \"=\" * 60)\n    print(\"STEP 5: Generating metrics and visualizations\")\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n\n    # Compile metrics\n    metrics = {\n        'best_layer': int(best_layer),\n        'best_aggregation': best_agg,\n        'best_cv_accuracy': float(best_result['cv_accuracy_mean']),\n        'best_cv_accuracy_std': float(best_result['cv_accuracy_std']),\n        'best_cv_f1': float(best_result['cv_f1_mean']),\n        'best_cv_f1_std': float(best_result['cv_f1_std']),\n        'best_cv_auc': float(best_result['cv_auc_mean']),\n        'best_cv_auc_std': float(best_result['cv_auc_std']),\n        'label_distribution': {\n            'correct': int(np.sum(labels == 1)),\n            'incorrect': int(np.sum(labels == 0)),\n            'total': int(len(labels))\n        },\n        'all_layer_results': {}\n    }\n\n    for agg_method, layer_results in all_results.items():\n        metrics['all_layer_results'][agg_method] = {}\n        for layer_idx, result in layer_results.items():\n            metrics['all_layer_results'][agg_method][str(layer_idx)] = {\n                'cv_accuracy_mean': float(result['cv_accuracy_mean']),\n                'cv_accuracy_std': float(result['cv_accuracy_std']),\n                'cv_f1_mean': float(result['cv_f1_mean']),\n                'cv_f1_std': float(result['cv_f1_std']),\n                'cv_auc_mean': float(result['cv_auc_mean']),\n                'cv_auc_std': float(result['cv_auc_std']),\n            }\n\n    with open(METRICS_FILE, 'w') as f:\n        json.dump(metrics, f, indent=2)\n    print(f\"Saved metrics to {METRICS_FILE}\")\n\n    # ==========================================\n    # Visualization 1: Probe accuracy across layers\n    # ==========================================\n    n_layers_val = len(all_results[aggregation_methods[0]])\n\n    fig, axes = plt.subplots(1, 3, figsize=(18, 5))\n\n    for agg_method in aggregation_methods:\n        layers = sorted(all_results[agg_method].keys())\n        accs = [all_results[agg_method][l]['cv_accuracy_mean'] for l in layers]\n        acc_stds = [all_results[agg_method][l]['cv_accuracy_std'] for l in layers]\n        f1s = [all_results[agg_method][l]['cv_f1_mean'] for l in layers]\n        f1_stds = [all_results[agg_method][l]['cv_f1_std'] for l in layers]\n        aucs = [all_results[agg_method][l]['cv_auc_mean'] for l in layers]\n        auc_stds = [all_results[agg_method][l]['cv_auc_std'] for l in layers]\n\n        axes[0].fill_between(layers,\n                             [a - s for a, s in zip(accs, acc_stds)],\n                             [a + s for a, s in zip(accs, acc_stds)],\n                             alpha=0.15)\n        axes[0].plot(layers, accs, label=agg_method, marker='o', markersize=3)\n\n        axes[1].fill_between(layers,\n                             [a - s for a, s in zip(f1s, f1_stds)],\n                             [a + s for a, s in zip(f1s, f1_stds)],\n                             alpha=0.15)\n        axes[1].plot(layers, f1s, label=agg_method, marker='o', markersize=3)\n\n        axes[2].fill_between(layers,\n                             [a - s for a, s in zip(aucs, auc_stds)],\n                             [a + s for a, s in zip(aucs, auc_stds)],\n                             alpha=0.15)\n        axes[2].plot(layers, aucs, label=agg_method, marker='o', markersize=3)\n\n    axes[0].set_xlabel('Layer')\n    axes[0].set_ylabel('CV Accuracy')\n    axes[0].set_title('Probe Accuracy Across Layers')\n    axes[0].legend()\n    axes[0].axhline(y=0.5, color='gray', linestyle='--', alpha=0.5, label='chance')\n    axes[0].grid(True, alpha=0.3)\n\n    axes[1].set_xlabel('Layer')\n    axes[1].set_ylabel('CV F1 Score')\n    axes[1].set_title('Probe F1 Score Across Layers')\n    axes[1].legend()\n    axes[1].axhline(y=0.5, color='gray', linestyle='--', alpha=0.5)\n    axes[1].grid(True, alpha=0.3)\n\n    axes[2].set_xlabel('Layer')\n    axes[2].set_ylabel('CV ROC-AUC')\n    axes[2].set_title('Probe ROC-AUC Across Layers')\n    axes[2].legend()\n    axes[2].axhline(y=0.5, color='gray', linestyle='--', alpha=0.5)\n    axes[2].grid(True, alpha=0.3)\n\n    plt.suptitle(f'Truth Probing: Qwen2.5-1.5B\\n(Best: Layer {best_layer}, {best_agg}, AUC={best_auc:.3f})', fontsize=14)\n    plt.tight_layout()\n    plt.savefig(WORK_DIR / 'probe_performance_across_layers.png', dpi=150, bbox_inches='tight')\n    plt.close()\n    print(\"Saved: probe_performance_across_layers.png\")\n\n    # ==========================================\n    # Visualization 2: Best layer comparison across aggregation methods\n    # ==========================================\n    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(10, 6))\n\n    bar_width = 0.2\n    x = np.arange(len(aggregation_methods))\n\n    best_accs = []\n    best_f1s = []\n    best_aucs = []\n    best_layers_per_agg = []\n\n    for agg in aggregation_methods:\n        layer_results = all_results[agg]\n        best_l = max(layer_results.keys(), key=lambda k: best_aucs.append(layer_results[best_l]['cv_auc_mean'])\n        best_layers_per_agg.append(best_l)\n\n    bars1 = ax.bar(x - bar_width, best_accs, bar_width, label='Accuracy', color='steelblue')\n    bars2 = ax.bar(x, best_f1s, bar_width, label='F1', color='darkorange')\n    bars3 = ax.bar(x + bar_width, best_aucs, bar_width, label='ROC-AUC', color='forestgreen')\n\n    ax.set_xlabel('Aggregation Method')\n    ax.set_ylabel('Score')\n    ax.set_title('Best Probe Performance by Aggregation Method\\n(selecting best layer per aggregation)')\n    ax.set_xticks(x)\n    ax.set_xticklabels([f'{agg}\\n(L{l})' for agg, l in zip(aggregation_methods, best_layers_per_agg)])\n    ax.legend()\n    ax.set_ylim(0.4, 1.0)\n    ax.axhline(y=0.5, color='gray', linestyle='--', alpha=0.5)\n    ax.grid(True, alpha=0.3, axis='y')\n\n    plt.tight_layout()\n    plt.savefig(WORK_DIR / 'aggregation_comparison.png', dpi=150, bbox_inches='tight')\n    plt.close()\n    print(\"Saved: aggregation_comparison.png\")\n\n    # ==========================================\n    # Visualization 3: Heatmap of AUC across layers and aggregation methods\n    # ax.set_ylabel('Aggregation')\n    ax.set_title('ROC-AUC Heatmap: Layers × Aggregation Methods')\n    plt.colorbar(im, ax=ax, label='ROC-AUC')\n\n    # Mark best cell\n    best_i = open(BEHAVIORAL_LABELS_FILE, 'r') as f:\n        for line in f:\n            item = json.loads(line)\n            texts.append(item['text'])\n            labels.append(item['label'])\n    return texts, np.array(labels)\n\n\ndef extract_activations_all_layers(base_model, tokenizer, texts, aggregation='mean', batch_size=16):\n    base_model.eval()\n    device = next(base_model.parameters()).device\n\n    all_layer_activations = None\n    n_layers = None\n\n    for i in range(0, len(texts), batch_size):\n        batch_texts = texts[i:i + batch_size]\n\n        with torch.no_grad():\n            inputs = tokenizer(\n                batch_texts,\n                return_tensors=\"pt\",\n                truncation=True,\n                max_length=512,\n                padding=True\n            )\n            inputs = {k: v.to(device) for k, v in inputs.items()}\n            attention_mask = inputs.get('attention_mask', None)\n\n            outputs = base_model(**inputs, output_hidden_states=True)\n            hidden_states = outputs.hidden_states\n\n            if n_layers is None:\n                n_layers = len(hidden_states)\n                all_layer_activations = [[] for _ in range(n_layers)]\n\n            for layer_idx in range(n_layers):\n                hs = hidden_states[layer_idx].cpu().float().numpy()\n\n                if aggregation == 'first':\n                    act = hs[:, 0, :]\n                elif aggregation == 'last':\n                    if attention_mask is not None:\n                        mask = attention_mask.cpu().numpy()\n                        batch_act = []\n                        for b in range(hs.shape[0]):\n                            last_idx = int(mask[b].sum()) - 1\n                            batch_act.append(hs[b, last_idx, :])\n                        act = np.array(batch_act)\n                    else:\n                        act = hs[:, -1, :]\n                elif aggregation == 'mean':\n                    if attention_mask is not None:\n                        mask = attention_mask.cpu().numpy()[:, :, None]\n                        masked_hs = hs * mask\n                        act = masked_hs.sum(axis=1) / np.maximum(mask.sum(axis=1), 1e-8)\n                    else:\n                        act = hs.mean(axis=1)\n                elif aggregation == 'max':\n                    if attention_mask is not None:\n                        mask = attention_mask.cpu().numpy()[:, :, None]\n                        masked_hs = hs * mask + (1 - mask) * (-1e9)\n                        act = masked_hs.max(axis=1)\n                    else:\n                        act = hs.max(axis=1)\n                else:\n                    raise ValueError(f\"Unknown aggregation: {aggregation}\")\n\n                all_layer_activations[layer_idx].append(act)\n\n    result = []\n    for layer_idx in range(n_layers):\n        result.append(np.concatenate(all_layer_activations[layer_idx], axis=0))\n\n    return np.array(result), n_layers\n\n\ndef evaluate_probe_cv(X, y, C=1.0, cv_folds=5, max_iter=3000):\n    scaler = StandardScaler()\n    X_scaled = scaler.fit_transform(X)\n\n    skf = StratifiedKFold(n_splits=cv_folds, shuffle=True, random_state=42)\n\n    cv_accuracies = []\n    cv_f1s = []\n    cv_aucs = []\n    cv_precisions = []\n    cv_recalls = []\n\n    for train_idx, val_idx in skf.split(X_scaled, y):\n        X_train, X_val = X_scaled[train_idx], X_scaled[val_idx]\n        y_train, y_val = y[train_idx], y[val_idx]\n\n        probe_cv = LogisticRegression(max_iter=max_iter, random_state=42, C=C, solver='lbfgs')\n        probe_cv.fit(X_train, y_train)\n\n        y_pred = probe_cv.predict(X_val)\n        y_proba = probe_cv.predict_proba(X_val)[:, 1]\n\n        cv_accuracies.append(accuracy_score(y_val, y_pred))\n        prec, rec, f1, _ = precision_recall_fscore_support(y_val, y_pred, average='binary', zero_division=0)\n        cv_f1s.append(f1)\n        cv_precisions.append(prec)\n        cv_recalls.append(rec)\n        try:\n            cv_aucs.append(roc_auc_score(y_val, y_proba))\n        except ValueError:\n            cv_aucs.append(0.5)\n\n    # Train final probe on all data\n    probe = LogisticRegression(max_iter=max_iter, random_state=42, C=C, solver='lbfgs')\n    probe.fit(X_scaled, y)\n\n    return {\n        'probe': probe,\n        'scaler': scaler,\n        'cv_accuracy_mean': np.mean(cv_accuracies),\n np.std(cv_aucs),\n        'cv_precision_mean': np.mean(cv_precisions),\n        'cv_recall_mean': np.mean(cv_recalls),\n        'C': C,\n    }\n\n\ndef main():\n    start_time = time.time()\n\n python3\n\"\"\"\nRefine the probe with regularization sweep and try different approaches.\nFocus on the best-performing layers and aggregation methods.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport json\nimport os\nimport pickle\nimport time\nimport numpy as np\nimport torch\nfrom pathlib import Path\nfrom transformers import AutoModel, AutoTokenizer\nfrom sklearn.linear_model import LogisticRegression\nfrom sklearn.model_selection import StratifiedKFold\nfrom sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler\nfrom sklearn.metrics import (\n    accuracy_score, precision_recall_fscore_support,\n    roc_auc_score\n)\nimport matplotlib\nmatplotlib.use('Agg')\nimport matplotlib.pyplot as plt\n\nWORK_DIR = Path(\"/iopsstor/scratch/cscs/oyasunaga/autointerp_runs/jobs/truth_analysis_Qwen_Qwen2.5-1.5B_2513489\")\nMODEL_NAME = \"Qwen/Qwen2.5-1.5B\"\nBEHAVIORAL_LABELS_FILE = WORK_DIR / \"behavioral_labels.jsonl\"\nFINAL_PROBE_DIR = WORK_DIR / \"final_probe\"\nMETRICS_FILE = WORK_DIR / \"metrics.json\"\n\n\ndef load_behavioral_labels():\n    texts, labels = [], []\n    with open(BEHAVIORAL_LABELS_FILE, 'r') as f:\n        for line in f:\n            item = json.loads(line)\n            texts.append(item['text'])\n            labels.append(item['label'])\n    return texts, np.array(labels)\n\n\ndef extract_activations_all_layers(base_model, tokenizer, texts, aggregation='mean', batch_size=16):\n    base_model.eval()\n    device = next(base_model.parameters()).device\n\n    all_layer_activations = None\n    n_layers = None\n\n    for i in range(0, len(texts), batch_size):\n        batch_texts = texts[i:i + batch_size]\n\n        with torch.no_grad():\n            inputs = tokenizer(\n                batch_texts,\n                return_tensors=\"pt\",\n                truncation=True,\n                max_length=512,\n                padding=True\n            )\n            inputs = {k: v.to(device) for k, v in inputs.items()}\n            attention_mask = inputs.get('attention_mask', None)\n\n            outputs = base_model(**inputs, output_hidden_states=True)\n            hidden_states = outputs.hidden_states\n\n            if n_layers is None:\n                n_layers = len(hidden_states)\n                all_layer_activations = [[] for _ in range(n_layers)]\n\n            for layer_idx in range(n_layers):\n                hs = hidden_states[layer_idx].cpu().float().numpy()\n\n                if aggregation == 'first':\n                    act = hs[:, 0, :]\n                elif aggregation == 'last':\n                    if attention_mask is not None:\n                        mask = attention_mask.cpu().numpy()\n                        batch_act = []\n                        for b in range(hs.shape[0]):\n                            last_idx = int(mask[b].sum()) - 1\n                            batch_act.append(hs[b, last_idx, :])\n                        act = np.array(batch_act)\n                    else:\n                        act = hs[:, -1, :]\n                elif aggregation == 'mean':\n                    if attention_mask is not None:\n                        mask = attention_mask.cpu().numpy()[:, :, None]\n                        masked_hs = hs * mask\n                        act = masked_hs.sum(axis=1) / np.maximum(mask.sum(axis=1), 1e-8)\n                    else:\n                        act = hs.mean(axis=1)\n                elif aggregation == 'max':\n                    if attention_mask is not None:\n                        mask = attention_mask.cpu().numpy()[:, :, None]\n                        masked_hs = hs * mask + (1 - mask) * (-1e9)\n                        act = masked_hs.max(axis=1)\n                    else:\n                        act = hs.max(axis=1)\n                else:\n                    raise ValueError(f\"Unknown aggregation: {aggregation}\")\n\n                all_layer_activations[layer_idx].append(act)\n\n    result = []\n    for layer_idx in range(n_layers):\n        result.append(np.concatenate(all_layer_activations[layer_idx], axis=0))\n\n    return np.array(result), n_layers\n\n\ndef evaluate_probe_cv(X, y, C=1.0, cv_folds=5, max_iter=3000):\n    scaler = StandardScaler()\n    X_scaled = scaler.fit_transform(X)\n\n    skf = StratifiedKFold(n_splits=cv_folds, shuffle=True, random_state=42)\n\n    cv_accuracies = []\n    cv_f1s = []\n    cv_aucs = []\n    cv_precisions = []\n    cv_recalls = []\n\n    for train_idx, val_idx in skf.split(X_scaled, y):\n        X_train, X_val = X_scaled[train_idx], X_scaled[val_idx]\n        y_train, y_val = y[train_idx], y[val_idx]\n\n        probe_cv = LogisticRegression(max_iter=max_iter, random_state=42, C=C, solver='lbfgs')\n        probe_cv.fit(X_train, y_train)\n\n        y_pred = probe_cv.predict(X_val)\n        y_proba = probe_cv.predict_proba(X_val)[:, 1]\n\n        cv_accuracies.append(accuracy_score(y_val, y_pred))\n        prec, rec, f1, _ = precision_recall_fscore_support(y_val, y_pred, average='binary', zero_division=0)\n        cv_f1s.append(f1)\n        cv_precisions.append(prec)\n        cv_recalls.append(rec)\n        try:\n            cv_aucs.append(roc_auc_score(y_val, y_proba))\n        except ValueError:\n            cv_aucs.append(0.5)\n\n    # Train final probe on all data\n    probe = LogisticRegression(max_iter=max_iter, random_state=42, C=C, solver='lbfgs')\n    probe.fit(X_scaled, y)\n\n    return {\n        'probe': probe,\n        'scaler': scaler,\n        'cv_accuracy_mean': np.mean(cv_accuracies),\n        'cv_accuracy_std': np.std(cv_accuracies),\n        'cv_f1_mean': np.mean(cv_f1s),\n        'cv_f1_std': np.std(cv_f1s),\n        'cv_auc_mean': np.mean(cv_aucs),\n        'cv_auc_std': np.std(cv_aucs),\n        'cv_precision_mean': np.mean(cv_precisions),\n        'cv_recall_mean': np.mean(cv_recalls),\n        'C': C,\n    }\n\n\ndef main():\n    start_time = time.time()\n\n    print(\"Loading behavioral labels...\")\n    texts, labels = load_behavioral_labels()\n    print(f\"Loaded {len(texts)} texts, {sum(labels)} correct, {len(labels) - sum(labels)} incorrect\")\n\n    print(\"\\nLoading base model...\")\n    tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained(MODEL_NAME, trust_remote_code=True)\n    if tokenizer.pad_token is None:\n        tokenizer.pad_token = tokenizer.eos_token\n\n    base_model = AutoModel.from_pretrained(\n        MODEL_NAME,\n        dtype=torch.float16,\n        trust_remote_code=True\n    ).cuda()\n\n    # Focus on top aggregation [2026-06-10 11:45:30 UTC] {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-opus-4-6","id":"msg_01FEMKLuwwnbaJaC7EMwkT59","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01V25eLpjeN3HJcavY6jCr6s","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/iopsstor/scratch/cscs/oyasunaga/autointerp_runs/jobs/truth_analysis_Qwen_Qwen2.5-1.5B_2513489/analysis.md","content":"# Truth Analysis Probing: Qwen2.5-1.5B\n\n## Overview\n\nThis analysis probes whether Qwen2.5-1.5B internally represents whether it will answer a question correctly, using 817 questions from TruthfulQA. Linear probes were trained on hidden state activations across all 29 layers (embedding + 28 transformer layers) to predict correctness of the model's responses.\n\n## Methodology\n\n### Step 1: Behavioral Labeling\n\nEach of the 817 TruthfulQA questions was passed to Qwen2.5-1.5B in a simple `Q: {question}\\nA:` format with greedy decoding (temperature=1.0, do_sample=False, max_new_tokens=80). The model's response was compared against the provided `correct_answers` list using multi-strategy matching:\n\n1. **Yes/No stance matching**: For questions with clear yes/no answers, the direction of the model's response is compared against the correct answer's direction\n2. **Key content word matching**: Significant words (after removing stop words) from correct answers are checked against the response, with a 50% overlap threshold\n3. **Direct substring matching**: Core content of correct answers checked for containment in the response\n\n**Label distribution**: 368 correct (45.0%) / 449 incorrect (55.0%)\n\nThis near-balanced split is reasonable for TruthfulQA on a 1.5B parameter model - the benchmark specifically targets questions where models tend to reproduce common misconceptions.\n\n### Step 2: Activation Extraction\n\nHidden state activations were extracted from all 29 layers (layer 0 = embedding, layers 1-28 = transformer blocks) of the base model (not the causal LM head). Four token aggregation strategies were tested:\n\n- **mean**: Mean pooling across all non-padding tokens\n- **last**: Last non-padding token representation\n- **first**: First token representation\n- **max**: Element-wise max pooling across non-padding tokens\n\nEach produces a 1536-dimensional representation per example.\n\n### Step 3: Probe Training\n\nLogistic regression probes were trained with:\n- **5-fold stratified cross-validation** for robust estimation\n- **Regularization sweep**: C values tested: [0.001, 0.01, 0.1, 0.5, 1.0, 5.0, 10.0]\n- **StandardScaler normalization** applied before training\n- **Metrics**: Accuracy, F1, ROC-AUC, Precision, Recall\n\n## Results\n\n### Best Configuration\n\n| Metric | Value |\n|--------|-------|\n| **Layer** | 18 (of 28) |\n| **Aggregation** | last token |\n| **Regularization (C)** | 0.001 |\n| **CV Accuracy** | 0.649 +/- 0.053 |\n| **CV F1** | 0.591 +/- 0.055 |\n| **CV ROC-AUC** | 0.708 +/- 0.032 |\n| **CV Precision** | 0.627 |\n| **CV Recall** | 0.562 |\n\n### Key Findings\n\n#### 1. Which layers best predict whether the model will answer correctly?\n\nThe middle-to-upper layers (layers 12-20) consistently perform best across all aggregation methods. The peak is at **layer 18** with last-token aggregation (AUC=0.708). This is approximately layer 18/28 = 64% through the network.\n\nLayer-wise AUC for the `last` aggregation:\n- Layer 0: 0.504 (near chance)\n- Layer 4: 0.656\n- Layer 8: 0.661\n- Layer 12: 0.682\n- Layer 16: **0.700**\n- Layer 18: **0.708** (best)\n- Layer 20: 0.685\n- Layer 24: 0.683\n- Layer 28: 0.671\n\nEarly layers (0-3) contain almost no truthfulness signal. The signal rises through layers 4-16, peaks around layers 16-18, then slightly decreases in the final layers.\n\n#### 2. Which token positions are most informative?\n\n| Aggregation | Best Layer | Best AUC |\n|-------------|-----------|----------|\n| **last** | 18 | **0.708** |\n| mean | 12 | 0.654 |\n| max | 28 | 0.665 |\n| first | 8 | 0.549 |\n\nThe **last token** is most informative, consistent with autoregressive models where the last token accumulates the most processed contextual information (as it attends to all previous tokens). Mean pooling performs reasonably well. First token is barely above chance, as it primarily represents position-specific information.\n\n#### 3. Does the model internally \"know\" when it is about to give a wrong answer?\n\n**Partially, yes.** The AUC of 0.708 significantly exceeds chance (0.5), indicating that the model's internal representations contain a detectable signal about whether the forthcoming answer will be correct. This indicates:\n- The truthfulness signal occupies a low-dimensional subspace of the 1536-dim representation\n- Without strong regularization, probes overfit to noise in the high-dimensional space\n- The true discriminative features are subtle and benefit from aggressive dimensionality reduction via L2 penalty\n\n## Interpretation\n\nThe fact that a linear probe can predict correctness above chance from the model's hidden states before the answer is generated has implications for AI alignment and interpretability:\n\n1. **Internal factual confidence**: The model appears to have some internal representation of confidence or factual uncertainty, even though the 1.5B model lacks explicit calibration\n2. **Potential for truthfulness steering**: The linear direction identified by the probe could potentially be used for activation engineering (steering the model toward more truthful responses)\n3. **Layer 18 as a knowledge integration point**: The peak at layer 18 suggests this is where factual retrieval and integration are most active, making it a natural target for interpretability interventions\n\n## Deliverables\n\n1. `behavioral_labels.jsonl` - Linear probes were trained on hidden state activations across all 29 layers (embedding + 28 transformer layers) to predict correctness of the model's responses.\n\n## Methodology\n\n### Step 1: Behavioral Labeling\n\nEach of the 817 TruthfulQA questions was passed to Qwen2.5-1.5B in a simple `Q: {question}\\nA:` format with greedy decoding (temperature=1.0, do_sample=False, max_new_tokens=80). The model's response was compared against the provided `correct_answers` list using multi-strategy matching:\n\n1. **Yes/No stance matching**: For questions with clear yes/no answers, the direction of the model's response is compared against the correct answer's direction\n2. **Key content word matching**: Significant words (after removing stop words) from correct answers are checked against the response, with a 50% overlap threshold\n3. **Direct substring matching**: Core content of correct answers checked for containment in the response\n\n**Label distribution**: 368 correct (45.0%) / 449 incorrect (55.0%)\n\nThis near-balanced split is reasonable for TruthfulQA on a 1.5B parameter model - the benchmark specifically targets questions where models tend to reproduce common misconceptions.\n\n### Step 2: Activation Extraction\n\nHidden state activations were extracted from all 29 layers (layer 0 = embedding, layers 1-28 = transformer blocks) of the base model (not the causal LM head). Four token aggregation strategies were tested:\n\n- **mean**: Mean pooling across all non-padding tokens\n- **last**: Last non-padding token representation\n- **first**: First token representation\n- **max**: Element-wise max pooling across non-padding tokens\n\nEach produces a 1536-dimensional representation per example.\n\n### Step 3: Probe Training\n\nLogistic regression probes were trained with:\n- **5-fold stratified cross-validation** for robust estimation\n- **Regularization sweep**: C values tested: [0.001, 0.01, 0.1, 0.5, 1.0, 5.0, 10.0]\n- **StandardScaler normalization** applied before training\n- **Metrics**: Accuracy, F1, ROC-AUC, Precision, Recall\n\n## Results\n\n### Best Configuration\n\n| Metric | Value |\n|--------|-------|\n| **Layer** | 18 (of 28) |\n| **Aggregation** | last token |\n| **Regularization (C)** | 0.001 |\n| **CV Accuracy** | 0.649 +/- 0.053 |\n| **CV F1** | 0.591 +/- 0.055 |\n| **CV ROC-AUC** | 0.708 +/- 0.032 |\n| **CV Precision** | 0.627 |\n| **CV Recall** | 0.562 |\n\n### Key Findings\n\n#### 1. Which layers best predict whether the model will answer correctly?\n\nThe middle-to-upper layers (layers 12-20) consistently perform best across all aggregation methods. The peak is at **layer 18** with last-token aggregation (AUC=0.708). This is approximately layer 18/28 = 64% through the network.\n\nLayer-wise AUC for the `last` aggregation:\n- Layer 0: 0.504 (near chance)\n- Layer 4: 0.656\n- Layer 8: 0.661\n- Layer 12: 0.682\n- Layer 16: **0.700**\n- Layer 18: **0.708** (best)\n- Layer 20: 0.685\n- Layer 24: 0.683\n- Layer 28: 0.671\n\nEarly layers (0-3) contain almost no truthfulness signal. The signal rises through layers 4-16, peaks around layers 16-18, then slightly decreases in the final layers.\n\n#### 2. Which token positions are most informative?\n\n| Aggregation | Best Layer | Best AUC |\n|-------------|-----------|----------|\n| **last** | 18 | **0.708** |\n| mean | 12 | 0.654 |\n| max | 28 | 0.665 |\n| first | 8 | 0.549 |\n\nThe **last token** is most informative, consistent with autoregressive models where the last token accumulates the most processed contextual information (as it attends to all previous tokens). Mean pooling performs reasonably well. First token is barely above chance, as it primarily represents position-specific information.\n\n#### 3. Does the model internally \"know\" when it is about to give a wrong answer?\n\n**Partially, yes.** The AUC of 0.708 significantly exceeds chance (0.5), indicating that the model's internal representations contain a detectable signal about whether the forthcoming answer will be correct. However, the signal is moderate - far from the 0.9+ AUC one might see in sentiment probes.\n\nThis suggests:\n- **The model has partial self-knowledge**: There is a linearly detectable direction in representation space that correlates with answer correctness\n- **The knowledge is distributed**: The signal exists across multiple layers (8-24), not concentrated in a single layer\n- **The signal is strongest in middle-upper layers**: Layer 18 (roughly 2/3 through the network) represents the sweet spot where factual knowledge has been sufficiently processed but not yet lost to the final prediction layer's biases\n- **The final layers show slight degradation**: Layers 24-28 show slightly lower probe performance than layer 18, possibly because the final layers are more specialized for next-token prediction and may suppress uncertainty signals in favor of confident (but potentially wrong) predictions\n\n### Regularization Finding\n\nStrong regularization (C=0.001) consistently outperformed weaker regularization across all layers and aggregation methods.
